Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau Struggles to Ban Tortoise Slaughter

No Government Ban Issued

Investigation and Prohibition for Sanitation Reasons

The Chinese Association for the Protection of Animals, based on reports from its members, stated that several small boats are constantly moored along the river near Xujiahui, Shanghai, specializing in catching and killing tortoises year-round, with the slaughter being especially severe during the autumn and winter. The killing involves cracking shells, digging out meat, and shedding fresh blood, a horrific sight. Although tortoises are small creatures and harmless to humans, and not a staple food, why not let them live and die freely? Therefore, the Association recently sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, requesting them to issue an order to strictly prohibit the slaughter to uphold benevolence and save all living beings. Details have been reported in this newspaper. We have learned that the Bureau responded to the Chinese Association for the Protection of Animals yesterday, stating: "Upon investigation, Buddhism values compassion and advocates abstaining from killing, the intention of which is undoubtedly commendable. However, in practice, it cannot be used as a basis for government orders. Philanthropists often spend money to buy turtles to release them, but many in society still enjoy eating them. Government agencies have always adopted a laissez-faire policy and have never issued a ban. Furthermore, the Xujiahui area of this city is where many Catholics reside, and most of them are very fond of eating tortoises. An abrupt prohibition would undoubtedly cause resentment. As for the blood and flesh and the swarms of mosquitoes and flies mentioned in your letter, if they affect public health, they will naturally be subject to prohibition. We intend to order the relevant Sixth District Second Precinct to investigate and handle the matter."

Young Man Swallows Half a Bottle of Lysol, Fortunately Rescued by a Tea Boy

Life Still Uncertain

At around 10 PM the day before yesterday, a young traveler arrived at the Hongyun Hotel on Haining Road and booked Room 19. He signed his name as Huang Chengji, 21 years old, from Wuxi, in the guest register. It is unknown what stimulation the young man suffered, but he developed suicidal thoughts. He immediately swallowed a bottle of Lysol he had brought with him in the room. Fortunately, the hotel tea boy, Lin Agao, caught a glimpse of this and immediately stepped forward to snatch it away. However, he had already consumed more than half of it. The tea boy immediately ran to the front desk and reported it, and they then reported it to the Hongkou Police Department. Detective Zhang Guisheng was dispatched to investigate and learned that the young man's name was Huang Yongjian. He was transported to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. He is currently receiving treatment, and his life is still uncertain. The detective repeatedly questioned him about the reason for his suicide attempt, but he refused to reveal the truth. The young man is of medium build, wearing a striped cloth jacket, striped cloth padded trousers, and running shoes. His appearance does not resemble that of a lower-class person.

Silver Dollar Exchange Rate Soars Amidst U.S. Silver Price Increase

The price of silver dollars in the local market has suddenly soared due to the influence of the United States raising silver prices. Yesterday, the listed exchange rate reached 3,190 cash coins per silver dollar, and 12.246 cents per double dime, which is a difference of more than 200 cash coins per dollar compared to the previous week. As a result, small-scale operators who carry goods by shoulder or hand are greatly affected. According to people in the money industry, the exchange rate may continue to rise.

A Female Buddhist Nun with Burned Hands and Feet Found on an Open Space in Hujia Wood Bridge

Recounts the Experience of Being Murdered After Regaining Consciousness

Dies Immediately After Recounting

The body of a female Buddhist nun was found on an open space on Quan Jia An Road in Hujia Wood Bridge, Hongkou, North Shanghai. Her hands and feet were charred. Villagers gathered around to watch. Officer Liu of the Fifth District Third Precinct rushed to investigate. Unexpectedly, the female nun suddenly regained consciousness. When asked about the cause, she groaned and said her name was Liu Fengshi, her husband's name was Liu Zigui, and she was from Funing. Last year, due to family reasons, she volunteered to be a vegetarian and chant Buddhist scriptures. Her husband sent her to Shanghai to become a nun at the Weishēng Temple in Hongkou. The abbess was named Li Guizhen. When she first came to Shanghai, her husband gave her more than 500 silver dollars to provide for her comfortable living. However, after several months, the abbess swindled her out of almost all of it and recently forced her to go out to solicit donations. However, as she was devoted to self-cultivation, she was not skilled in this area, so she refused. The old nun resented this, severely punished her, and poured anesthetic medicine on her, causing her to become unconscious. She did not know how she ended up here. She was in excruciating pain, and her hands and feet were burned. After speaking, her breath was faint. When they tried to ask more questions, she died immediately. Officer Liu immediately reported to the chief and ordered a thorough investigation. There was no Weishēng Temple by that name, so it must be another name. He ordered the neighborhood chief to report to the local court and appoint Prosecutor Xie.

Wheel of Fortune Gambling Den Busted in a Grand Building on Avenue Haig

Comparable to the One Set Up by Cassia in the Past

Operated by Jewish White Russian Yao Kesutuoto

Brazilian Consul Actually Sent a Letter Claiming He Was Brazilian

But Yao's Nationality Has Been Verified by the Police Authority

| Result: Yao Detained, Hearing Postponed |

The grand building at No. 1475, Lane 1, Avenue Haig, is the property of the British firm, Terry & Co. Last autumn, Zhang Chengde rented the house from the firm, signing a lease and paying a monthly rent of over 280 yuan. No one initially knew what he was using it for, but soon the police authorities discovered that a very large Wheel of Fortune gambling den was set up inside. The operator was a Jewish White Russian named Yao Kesutuoto (Y. Shutte). Zhang Chengde, the tenant, was merely a figurehead. The equipment inside the gambling den was comparable to the one

Brazilian Cassia

Organized on Tongfu Road in the past. Therefore, every night, dozens of gamblers frequented it, with at least forty or fifty, even on frosty, snowy, or rainy nights. The gamblers were a mix of Chinese and foreigners, men and women. However, there were more Chinese. The amount of winnings and losses and the richness of the prizes were said to be astounding. Yao started operating in August of last year and has been doing so until now. The amount of illegal income is considerable. The police authorities had heard about it early on, but they continued to investigate secretly because they had not fully understood its essence. Every night, detectives were dispatched to the vicinity of the den to

Observe Gamblers Entering and Exiting

Recently, they went a step further, selecting detectives and having them disguised as gamblers, mixing into the den. Only then did they get a complete picture and know for sure that it was set up by Yao. On Friday of the previous week, they requested arrest warrants and search warrants from the First Special District Court. They originally planned to secretly raid and arrest that night. Unexpectedly, the gambling lord was extremely resourceful and found out in advance. Gambling was stopped that night, and Yao temporarily hid, causing the detectives to make a futile trip. Fearing that this would cause alarm and allow the gambling lord to escape, they immediately investigated

The Whereabouts of Yao's Hiding Place

They soon learned that he was hiding at No. 504, Broadway Road. Hui Sikaosi, a Western detective from the Jing'an Temple Police Station, went to the address with a Chinese detective on the morning of the day before yesterday at 11 AM and arrested Yao. Then, at 4:30 PM, they searched the gambling den again and confiscated chips for Wheel of Fortune gambling and nine dozen pencils used for counting, paper, rubber bands, tablecloths, and other items, which were all taken back to the police station. Upon learning of this, the Consul General of Brazil stationed in Shanghai prepared two official letters, one addressed to President Guo of the First Special District Court and the other to the Presiding Judge of the Criminal Court, and

Personally Brought the Two Letters to the Court

To prove that Yao was a Brazilian national. As it was a holiday that day, the Consul left the letters and left. However, the police authorities had already investigated and clarified the nationality of the gambling lord with the Foreign Nationals Registration Office of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau. He was indeed a Jewish White Russian, with his own photo and that of his wife, as well as his signature as proof. Therefore, yesterday morning, the police station sent Yao to the First Special District Court and charged him with the crime of running a gambling den and skimming profits, violating Article 280 of the Criminal Law. Judge Wu Xiangzu presided over the interrogation. Bai Taili, the secretary of the Brazilian consulate, was sent to the court to observe. First, Ru BaoYi and Qian Xunjiu, lawyers for the police station, stated the process of the police station's investigation of the case, and

This Trial Arrested the Defendant

The situation. Next, the Western detective in charge reported the arrest of the defendant and the search of the gambling den, presenting each of the confiscated exhibits to the court. Judge Wu then questioned the defendant. Unexpectedly, the defendant was arrogant and claimed that he was a Brazilian national and did not want to speak in a Chinese court. If they wanted him to confess, they had to send him to the Brazilian consulate, which was purely empty talk with no evidence provided to prove that he was a Brazilian national. Therefore, at the end, the lawyer for the police station stated that the defendant's attitude in court was illegal. However, the case still needed to be postponed, and they requested that the defendant be detained. The court approved the request and ordered the defendant to be detained for a later hearing. It is said that in order to make the judge understand the contents of the gambling den, the police station planned to ask Judge Wu to conduct an on-site inspection.

Inspectors and forensic examiners arrived at the scene and determined that the deceased was a woman about 20 years old and had died from burns. They filled out the coroner's report, took photos, and the hall took charge of the body for encoffinment. An immediate investigation revealed that there was only one Lianhua Nunnery in Hongkou, with the abbess being a Cantonese woman named Shun Jin, and there were no nuns. Therefore, they could not find any leads. They were ordered to continue the investigation and apprehension.

Death of Mr. Qin Lizhai, Staff Member of This Newspaper

Mr. Qin Lizhai, a staff member of this newspaper, was the son of Mr. Pingfu, a veteran in the newspaper industry. He joined the newspaper in 1922, responsible for translating foreign news. He was diligent and hardworking. In his spare time, he also translated foreign telegrams for the National Society and occasionally contributed to travel magazines. Mr. Qin was usually quiet and rarely smiled, but he was sincere and honest in dealing with people. He was also very frugal and did not indulge in any worldly pleasures. He was respected by his colleagues. During the January 28th Incident, Mr. Qin Lizhai Image

He lived in Zhabei and was trapped in the siege, experiencing great hardship before reaching safety. Mr. Qin was already weak, and this ordeal made him even weaker. In recent years, he suffered from stomach problems, which came and went. However, he always forced himself to work and never slackened. In January of this year, his body finally gave out, and he had to take leave to rest. Unexpectedly, after more than a month of treatment, it was ineffective, and he suddenly passed away on the night of the 25th of this month, at the age of 40. He leaves behind three children. His death is mourned by his colleagues, and the translation community has lost a good talent, which is deeply regrettable.

Three Suicides

Social Pathologies... Cause for Concern

Drinking Poison: Gao Chunsheng from Taizhou, 32 years old, ran a mat shop with partners at No. 173, North Henan Road, for many years. Gao was in charge of the shop's affairs. In recent years, the shop's business has been very slow, and they have been experiencing financial difficulties. The day before yesterday, Gao became worried about this and developed suicidal thoughts. After dinner, he secretly swallowed Lysol. His brother, Gao Qinsheng, caught a glimpse of this, but it was too late. He immediately accompanied him to Tongren Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective, and he soon died. The hospital reported to the Huishi Police Station, and Detective Sun Changsheng went to investigate and then had the body taken to the Feilun Road morgue for an autopsy.

Hanging: Wang Shanga, a 19-year-old from Nanjing, had been an apprentice at the Shunfuchang coppersmith shop opened by Zhou Shengfu at No. 950, Zhoujiazui Road, for two years. The shop was divided into two sections: copper drawing and coppersmithing. Wang usually worked in the copper drawing section. However, the shop owner, seeing that there were not enough people in the coppersmithing section, transferred Wang to fill the gap. Wang was very dissatisfied with this and became resentful. The morning before last, he suddenly developed suicidal thoughts and, taking advantage of the lack of preparation, went to the workshop and hanged himself. When the shop owner caught a glimpse of this, he immediately cut him down, but it was too late. Only a breath of life remained. He reported it to the Huishan Police Station, and Detective Wang Tongpo went to investigate and took the apprentice to the hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and he soon died. The body was taken to the Feilun Road morgue for an autopsy.

Swallowing Red Pills: Liu Fenggao from Yancheng, 30 years old, lost his parents when he was young and was raised by his uncle, Chen Shengkang. Chen ran a stove shop at No. 128, Yucai Road, Xiangyan Bridge, for a living. Liu also helped his uncle there. Last year, in November of the lunar calendar, Chen married Sun, a woman from the same town, to Liu. At around 3 AM the day before yesterday, Liu got up for work and asked his wife to bring him a pair of socks to wear. However, she refused, causing an argument. Liu suddenly became resentful of this and developed suicidal thoughts. He went out alone that day, bought two yuan's worth of red pills, brought them back, and secretly swallowed them. When Chen noticed, he transported him to Tongren Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective, and he soon died. The hospital reported to the Hongkou Police Station, and Detective Zhang Guisheng went to investigate and then had the body taken to the Feilun Road morgue for an autopsy. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court received a report and appointed Prosecutor Guo Wei, along with forensic doctor Wei Ligong and clerk Wang Zuyi, to come to the morgue and verify that the body was indeed that of Liu. They then ordered the family members to sign separate guarantees and take the body back for burial.

The inventor hopes the government will approve it soon

After the successful invention of the water-powered motor (i.e., self-powered engine) by Chinese, it was twice submitted to the central government last year and recently for approval to protect patent rights. Details have been reported in newspapers. Recently, it was rumored that the inventors, Chen Dan and Liang, were planning to cooperate with foreigners or sell the entire machinery to foreigners due to circumstances and economic difficulties. A reporter from the Ri Ri News specifically inquired about Chen and Liang yesterday. According to Mr. Chen, the rumor of cooperating with foreigners was not without reason. Before the motor was successfully invented in the year before last, foreigners had come to discuss buying the drawings at a high price. In the spring of last year, a certain foreigner was willing to provide financial assistance and have the invention rights transferred. However, we were unwilling to let the glory of the Chinese people flow into foreign lands, so we refused sternly. Recently, I was forced by economic circumstances. In the past, I failed more than 100 times in inventing this motor. My personal and family assets have been consumed by no less than tens of thousands. Therefore, I finally submitted it to the government again, requesting assistance and earnestly hoping that the government would reply soon. If the government still hesitates and ignores it, then as a last resort, I may cooperate with foreigners. Recently, foreigners have been coming to the factory preparation office one after another to inquire, which shows that foreigners are paying close attention to this invention.

The Number of Kerosene Imports in the Last Five Years Is Shocking

According to the International Trade Bureau, kerosene is one of the fuels relied upon by families and industries. Since China has no kerosene mines to supply itself, it relies on imports from the United Kingdom and the United States. British Asiatic Petroleum Co., Ltd. and American Mobil Oil Co., Ltd. sell kerosene worth tens of millions of dollars in China every year. After China resumed diplomatic relations with the Soviet Union, the Oil Across the Land Company also competed to dump kerosene in China. Therefore, since 1932, the number of kerosene imports has increased by about onefold compared to five years ago. The statistics of kerosene imports in the last five years are listed below: 1929: 55,177,498 customs taels; 1930: 54,864,546 customs taels; 1931: 64,549,371 customs taels; 1932: 94,244,822 national currency; 1933: 87,450,738 national currency.

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Recovers the Right to Supply Electricity to Dinghai Island

Dinghai Island was originally a beach reclaimed by the Huangpu Bureau. The electricity there was supplied by the Shanghai Electric Company. The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities believed that since the area belonged to the Chinese Concession but was supplied with electricity by a foreign company across the border, it was detrimental to sovereignty. After negotiations with the Huangpu Bureau in July 1931, it was changed to Chinese-owned electrical power. The Zhabei Water and Electricity Company was ordered to lay submarine cables and supply electricity. This equipment project has now been completed, and the company began supplying electricity on January 29th of this year. The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities has also installed streetlights on the main roads, which residents say is very convenient.

Residents in the City Center Request Electricity Supply Lines

No Fees Required

In order to promote the prosperity of the city center, the Shanghai Municipal Government has been making unremitting efforts to promote construction in the area. Regarding electricity supply, the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities has already agreed with the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, which supplies electricity to the area, that no fees will be charged for residents in the area who request electricity supply lines, and the Shanghai Municipal Government will guarantee interest. The method is that the Shanghai Municipal Government will guarantee within five years that the annual electricity fee will be sufficient to cover 12% of the actual construction cost of the lines. If there is a shortfall, the Shanghai Municipal Government will make up for it. Therefore, it is extremely convenient for residents in the area to request electricity supply lines.

The Mechanical Industry Association Produces and Distributes Safety Warning Posters for Factories

The Shanghai Mechanical Chinese Goods Factory Joint Association recently noted that it is not possible for factories to improve safety equipment without sufficient financial resources and talent. However, it is easy for factories to hang special signs in machine rooms, raw material rooms, and manufacturing rooms to warn workers to avoid major disasters caused by carelessness. Thousands of iron signs have been produced with warning words such as "Beware of Fire" and "Beware of Danger," as well as simple and easy-to-understand designs of skull and bones, etc. They have begun printing and will be distributed to member factories to reduce disasters.

Sichuan Gang Resists Price Increases of Various Ships, Plans to Suspend Commercial Goods for Two Months

New Alliance Charter of Various Shipping Companies

Trial Run for Two Months After Signing

The Sichuan River shipping companies in Shanghai are proceeding with a cooperative alliance to increase water freight by 100%, which has aroused the opposition of the entire Sichuan Gang, preparing for two months of sacrifice to resist the various Sichuan ships. The alliance contract has been signed. The reporter will investigate and report the follow-up news of this matter as follows:

Chinese Ships Suffer Losses in Cooperation

The initiators of this Sichuan River shipping alliance are Jiangjiang, Taikoo, Minsheng, and Jardine Matheson, while Sanbei and Guangyao have also joined the scope of this cooperation. At that time, the Chinese shipping companies proposed that the Wukui Line and Wanxian Port business has always been operated only by Chinese ships, and foreign ships are not allowed to go there, and British ships cannot sail to Wanxian. The business in these two places is usually not included in the scope of public sharing. This time, the representatives of the various companies in Shanghai agreed on the same, and Wanxian Wukui was also included in the public sharing regulations. The contract has been signed. According to people in the Shanghai shipping industry, except for Minsheng, the Chinese shipping companies have suffered losses in this Sichuan shipping alliance. The normally profitable Wukui Wanhang business has also been publicly allocated, which is not in the interest of Chinese ships.

China Merchants Did Not Join

China Merchants Bureau originally had a ship, the Emei, in the Sichuan River. Since it had an accident in July of last year, it has not been salvaged. The reefs on the bottom of the ship have been blasted. After the spring flood, it is hoped that it can be towed to Shanghai for major repairs. Since the Emei accident, the China Merchants Bureau has not had any ships running in the Sichuan River. Even if the Emei is repaired, it will be changed to the Jinghan express line. There will be no ships running in the Sichuan River for the time being. Therefore, the China Merchants Bureau did not join this alliance cooperation.

Alliance to Trial Run for Two Months

The alliance contract has been signed by various public companies such as Jiangjiang, Minsheng, Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, Sanbei, and Guangyao. The freight for loading goods is increased by 100% according to the original price rate. Cotton has been increased to 24 yuan per piece. Piece goods and other goods must be increased to 80 yuan per ton. The weight and size of other groceries are particularly serious. The increase in the price of goods this time is really unexpected. The shipping companies believe that the atmosphere of the merchants is not good, so they have decided to implement the alliance for two months on a trial basis.

Sichuan Gang Prepares to Sacrifice

The various merchants of the Sichuan Gang in Shanghai believe that the increase in freight by the shipping companies this time is too great. After repeated meetings, it was agreed that the actual receipt for each piece of cotton was only eight yuan, and now it has increased by two-thirds. Groceries must also be charged according to gross weight, which is too much of a loss. They have repeatedly requested a reduction, but it has been rejected by the shipping companies. The various merchants of the Sichuan Gang have jointly decided that during the two-month trial period of this newly established alliance, they will bear the pain and suspend the business of commercial goods entering Sichuan for two months. After the two-month period expires, if the shipping companies can improve the methods, they will resume commercial transportation at that time. Otherwise, they will discuss a proper strategy.

Rent Dispute in Xicheng Lane, French Concession

The City Federation Branch Issued a Declaration Yesterday

Announcing a Rent Reduction for All

Due to opposition from tenants of Xicheng Lane on Malong Road in the French Concession against the landlord's imposition of harsh contracts, a large number of tenants were subjected to property seizures, causing public outrage. The Xicheng Lane Branch of the Fourth District Division of the Shanghai Special District Second City Federation was organized to collectively respond to the situation. Yesterday, they issued a declaration, tearfully pleading for assistance from all sectors. They also notified everyone to abide by the proposed rent reduction measures. The details are as follows:

Declaration

To All Organizations and Citizens of All Roads and Lanes in This City:

We are writing to inform you that our members all reside in houses in Xicheng Lane on Malong Road in the French Concession. These houses belong to the former General Commander of the Five Provinces Allied Forces, Sun Chuanfang, and their rental management has long been entrusted to the Yipin Bank. The tenants have lived here peacefully for eight years. Unexpectedly, the owner recently transferred the rental management rights to himself, under the name of Yiyuan Company. In January, they notified the tenants and imposed an illegal, one-sided contract. At the same time, rental collectors were forcing the collection of rent managed by Yipin, not allowing any arrears. Since the January 28th Incident, many tenants have had rent arrears of two or three months due to the economic downturn. The landlord ignored everything and insisted on full payment, using extremely aggressive methods. As a result, many tenants had to sell or pawn their belongings to pay. However, a few tenants who rely on their daily income for survival and are now facing the Lunar New Year season find it difficult to repay immediately. Even after pleading with the rental collectors for time or offering to pay half, they were ignored. Without providing written notices or summonses to the court, the landlord resorted to his old tricks of military oppression, falsely suing the tenants in court and implementing provisional attachment, sealing the houses of thirteen tenants. Amidst the current rent reduction movement, the landlord has uniquely created an illegal rental contract to revise rental prices and satisfy his desire to increase rent. He has also imposed harsh conditions, allowing arbitrary eviction. The tenants, unable to withstand this oppression, have no choice but to unite to seek common security. We sincerely hope that people from all walks of life will empathize with our plight, uphold justice, and provide assistance. Society will be fortunate. We hereby issue this declaration, hoping for your public consideration.

Notice to All

Regarding the matter of issuing a notice: Our association has been established, and executive officers have been elected to be responsible for handling negotiations. From now on, this association will implement resolutions separately based on decisions made at general meetings. The matters that must be observed and noted are hereby notified as follows: (1) Do not privately sign any illegal contracts with the landlord. If a contract has already been signed, report it to this association for a declaration of invalidity. If a contract has not been signed, submit the contract to this association. (2) The rent reduction issue in this lane will follow the rent reduction measures resolved by the Shanghai Rent Reduction Association, paying rent at 80% of the original amount. Until a satisfactory resolution is reached, all rents should be deposited individually at the Continental Bank on Xiafei Road to prevent the landlord from using it as an excuse. (3) Print rent investigation forms and covenants, and each person should fill them out and sign them. (4) If there is any oppression by the landlord, please report it to this association immediately for negotiation. (5) Everyone must strictly comply with the above measures without error. This notice is hereby issued.

Ma Hongdao, a Muslim Student Returning From Turkey, Will Tour and Lecture

Ma Hongdao, a Muslim (i.e., Islamic) student who has completed his studies in Turkey and returned to China, made the following statement yesterday: There are many "Islamic" Muslims in our country, and there are also many famous scholars. However, due to the oppression of autocratic emperors, the thinking of "Islamic" Muslims has changed. It seems that the country is the country, and religion is religion. They still have a twelve-point faith in religion, but they have an indifferent attitude towards the country. As long as I can live, no matter what happens to the country, it is up to fate. This kind of psychology of believing in religion but not loving the country is a big mistake. We should expand the psychology of believing in religion and extend it to the country. If we only care about religion and not the country, it is like the Buddhist places where chanting scriptures and praying are the way of life. Their cultural decline has reached its extreme, which looks very dangerous. Mr. Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People ultimately lead to government of the people, by the people, and for the people, and even to the path of a world commonwealth. This is to teach all Chinese people to do Chinese affairs together, to start with local autonomy and extend it to party affairs and government. Muhammad said in his holy decree, "Love of country is a part of faith." The Quran says, "Do not shed blood on the ground." In other words, Muhammad taught us to love our country, which is to be a complete Muslim. The deep meaning of the Quran is to teach us not to kill each other, but to pay attention to group life and go to the path of perfection. All "Islamic" Muslims are based on abiding by the Holy Decree and the Quran. Saying this, we will certainly correct the wrong psychology, eliminate foreign troubles, and eradicate internal worries. We must fight with the spirit of Turkey and Germany. In our country, there are "Islamic" Muslims with this kind of spirit, such as Zheng He of the former Ming Dynasty, Zuo Baogui and Ma Fulu of the former Qing Dynasty, and An Dexin, who passed away not long ago. These people all showed great fearless spirit and sacrificed themselves to win glory for the nation. Having seen this, Hongdao returned to China and gathered three or five like-minded people, hoping to visit all the religious relatives in the country in person after returning to China, planning to start from Nanjing, go north through Tianjin-Pukou, then go south through Pinghan, and return to Beijing along the Yangtze River, making a small-scale tour. On the one hand, he will offer his experiences to the religious compatriots, and on the other hand, he wants to know the current situation of the religious compatriots in various places. Since we are a nation in the world, the Chinese nation, we should rise up and cooperate so that we will not be oppressed by others. I hope that you religious relatives will help and guide as much as possible with everything you hope for.

Reading Q & A

Where Should One Start When Studying International Issues? (1)

Reading Guidance:

How fortunate I am to have found reading guidance in the mist! Therefore, I dare to present the questions I have accumulated over time to you gentlemen, hoping that you will provide open and concrete answers.

Before presenting my questions, I should briefly describe my life to seek your guidance. I am the son of a businessman, and also engaged in agriculture as a sideline. In recent years, affected by the bankruptcy of the rural economy, the business closed down long ago, and the land was also sold. What was originally more than twenty acres is now used to maintain life, which is the old debt remaining after the business closed down; therefore, the issue of livelihood is a problem that I urgently need to solve. I am currently a third-year student in a normal school's advanced program. The pain of unemployment is approaching, so my future is not optimistic.

Gentlemen, this is who I am. Next, I will talk about what I like to study. Although I am involved in normal school, I like to study international issues. The purpose is to explore the dynamic questions of international politics and economics from practical problems, in order to recognize future trends. However, I do not like foreign languages and have no knowledge of economics.

The materials I used to study were of two types, namely reading newspapers and various magazines. I am well aware that these two materials are very lacking, but I have no suitable person to guide me and am restricted by economic conditions, so I cannot buy more complete and expensive books, so I have to do it this way, until now, two difficulties have arisen: the information published in newspapers is unsystematic, and I cannot find the main factors causing certain problems, only the arrangement of some facts, and the truth is still questionable. (2) Reading magazines is also full of hearsay, and there is very little volatilization about the inside of the facts, and the reasons they hold are not much different, the only difference is the order of publication, the issue of time. These two mistakes prove that the price I paid for the time I spent before was empty! At the same time, I also feel the difficulty of cognitive ability. This has to be a reorganization, so the following questions arise:

A. Should a person in my living situation study international issues? Can I study it?

B. Where should one start when studying international issues?

C. How can I develop correct cognitive ability?

D. Can a person who does not understand foreign languages and has no knowledge of economics satisfy my desire to study international issues? If not, how can I satisfy it?

E. If I want to study economics, where should I start?

The above questions all urgently need your concrete answers. I can only wait for your instructions.

Chunqiu

Three Regrets

— Yanqiao

Song Yu Wenbao said: "I have three regrets, one is no son, two is no help, and three is no accomplishment. Holding this bitter heart, I entertain myself with words. I have already stopped writing in this record, and I will sing long to tie it together. It is laughable that spring silkworms are so foolish, working hard every year for others? It is just like a poor woman flying her shuttle, and she has never had anything to wear." This was inscribed on the back of his book "Blowing Sword Record." It was honest in his original intention. Only with these three regrets could the "Blowing Sword Record" be written. If he had a son, help, and accomplishment, I am afraid there would be no "Blowing Sword Record." Without the "Blowing Sword Record," who would know that there was a Yu Wenbao? So he said three regrets, I think it can be without regrets, because people leave a name after death, leopards leave their skin after death, abundant in this, stingy in that, why not be content with yourself?

Moreover, the three regrets he said are not enough to be considered regrettable, because Han Tuozhou said: "Gaining an official position satisfies everything, and having no son is easy for one's body." If the son is unfilial and brings shame to his parents, it is certainly regrettable. Even from breastfeeding to getting married, it takes a lot of trouble and hard work, which may not be pleasant. As for no help, it is probably because there are no close friends. Someone used to say, "Having a confidant can be without regrets." The help of friends is indeed indispensable in life. However, in addition to the help of friends, there are other aids, or beyond friends, such as the most authoritative and powerful attraction that is enough to influence the world. Mr. Yu's regret of no help, I do not know whether it includes all these aids. With help, it is easy to have accomplishments, so his third regret and second regret are mutually reinforcing. Taking a step back, Mr. Yu's words have been passed down to this day, which can be considered an accomplishment. This shows that his three regrets are really nothing to regret, what regrets are there!

The poor woman flies the shuttle, without a single thread, but it is the most common view of life, whether there are sons, help, or accomplishments, in the end there is still nothing. Materialist historians can see through it, like the predecessors said, "Have wine today, get drunk today, worry about tomorrow without money." Only today, without asking about tomorrow, is a great thought, and this thought is also the motor of all careers." Qian Muzhai took off his boots and wanted to throw himself into the water to die for his country, but he felt too cold, so he shrank his feet and stood up, wearing simple clothes and carrying food and drink to welcome the king's army. He has a concept of tomorrow in his heart.

Today, there is nothing else to regret, only one regret, which is the same in everyone's heart, is "no money." Even those who have money still regret that they don't have enough, or they and those who really have no money hold the same regret for the rest of their lives.

Losing a Son

— Zuo Yun

"Nothing is more heartbreaking than losing a son," this is indeed true, I really feel it now.

A good and healthy child is suddenly lost, after his parents have raised him for many years, kissed him, and regarded him as a second life, how heartbroken must the parents be?

Therefore, I just want to write out the following facts. In fact, my mood is under this great blow, and I cannot summarize this chaotic situation.

When the child's face turned pale and his body temperature gradually dropped, his mother still did not know to give up trying to save this little life, and tried her best to pray for God's blessing. Seeing this miserable and pitiful scene, I had to tell my wife: "The child is finished."

My wife woke up as if from a big dream, and at the same time screamed and fell into another dream, stiffly falling on the floor. At this time, the muscles all over my body were also soft and limp. Regret, decadence, sadness, and pain all came together. After rational control one by one, I took care of the child's funeral and comforted my wife, and then I was taken by my friends to the road for a walk.

The defect of mood cannot be compensated. This stimulation has completely submerged my heart. I don't believe that this healthy child is lost. I think this is a dream. When I wake up, my good child still exists. Who can believe that this healthy child will die? Who can believe it?

In this way, whether I am walking, sitting, or sleeping, as long as I am surrounded by a quiet space alone, this thought will come: "My child is not dead, right?" If reason tells me the truth, a chill will come and suffocate this thought. However, what follows is the trembling of the heart and the constant reflection of the child's life fragments.

The child is dead, and all the child's actions have become the object of remembrance. And my child, he is equipped with health and wisdom, so his actions are even more called me to remember, and my pain of losing a son is naturally strengthened.

Before, I had comforted my friend: "What does it matter to lose a child?" If someone comforts me like this now, I will definitely give him a strong revulsion, seeing that life must be experienced.

I have deeply tasted the grief of losing a son, so I know that the heartache of a person who loses a son cannot be matched by any other tragedy.

Whenever a New Book is Bought

— Dingming

New clothes are lovely, because after all, they are different from old clothes, and they can add a lot of spirit invisibly! As the saying goes: "People depend on clothes, horses depend on saddles!" Although divine steeds are trapped between troughs and stables, but "thousand-mile horses are often available, but Bole is not often available!" Like Wang Meng, who "wore rough clothes to visit, and talked while stroking lice" to Fu Jian, and Fan Wenzhenggong, who "the scholars changed their clothes to come out, but Zhongyan was as usual," how many people can there be in the world who are indifferent to material things and do not pay attention to appearance? It is enough to see that new clothes are universal and valuable!

The spiritual food of life - new books, are also like this!

Of course, opening the books, both Chinese and foreign, there are many smart and wise geniuses and what prodigies, however, without new books as a fuse, how can they ignite their dazzling sparks of knowledge, how can they develop their great mines of thought fuel?

Loving new books, buying new books, I have simply become a habit: if I have two smelly copper coins by my side, I will buy them all when I go to the bookstore; sometimes when I see a new book, I don't have money to buy it, I always go home with infinite sadness; but whenever I get a new book:

(1) First, I roughly flip through it with my eyes, to see if the words are beautiful? Are the illustrations exquisite? Or is the printing and binding solid and beautiful? Conduct a second aesthetic review, and then multiply and divide it with the price.

(2) Look at the catalog, how is the outline? How are the details? Close the book and think silently: What is the content of this book? (Actually, you don't need to close your eyes!) Guess the riddle once or twice.

(3) In the beginning of the new book, or the beginning of each chapter, first look at the first paragraph, and then cover it up and think about what kind of theories will be in the following; it seems that this book is my teacher, sitting upright and examining me orally.

(4) Like the third view, but turn the head around, first look at the lower paragraph, and then think about what is the meaning of the upper paragraph? In this way, after reading half a paragraph and thinking about half a paragraph. At first, nine out of ten guesses are wrong, but later they are still pertinent; I feel very rich and interesting, and get the benefit of observation invisibly.

(5) Sometimes I read a few paragraphs of a new book and insert it on the bookshelf, it is simply: "There are those who cannot see each other for thirty-six years!"

The above is my treatment method for new books I bought; may I ask another unfamiliar self-taught comrade how to deal with newly bought books?

Northeast Fourth Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Fourth: Drinking Wine and Passing Food, Reveling and Containing Farewell Tears, Burning the Lamp to Warm the Dream, Singing Softly to Spend the Long Night

As Guizhi spoke, she took the noodles to the kitchen. On the small coal stove, there was a kettle, and the kettle was tinkling, almost ready to boil, so she sat on a low chair by the stove, quietly waiting for the water to boil. Half-sideways, she propped her head with one hand and looked at the flame diagonally. I don't know why, a burst of heartache, two lines of tears rolled straight down from her pink face. She was staring at the fire in a daze, even though tears were streaming down her cheeks, she didn't care, just staring in a daze. Only when the boiling water rushed the pot lid, and with a puff, splashed the flames and released green flames, did she wake up in shock, quickly wipe away her tears, and carry the kettle into the room. As soon as she stepped into the room, she smiled at Ziqiang: If I'm not here to support you, you can't sing, right? Ziqiang smiled: My play, I can only sing and listen to myself. Guizhi made tea, cleaned up the bowls and chopsticks, took Ziqiang's hand, and sat down on a chair together. She smiled and said: I have a fresh little song, called "Persuading Husband to Improve," sing it for you to listen to, okay? Ziqiang held her hand with one hand and patted the back of her hand with the other, and said with a smile: Good, good, good! You just sing it. If I have anything to improve, after listening to your words, I can also improve it. Guizhi took two sips of the teacup, put down the teacup, smiled slightly at Ziqiang, and was about to open her mouth to sing, when suddenly a burst of alarm clock sounds came from the clothes on the hanger. Guizhi's face suddenly changed, and she grasped Ziqiang's hand and looked at his face. Ziqiang said: What time did you set the alarm clock to? Guizhi answered in a very miserable voice: It was originally set at five thirty. Ziqiang stood up and said: I have to leave at six o'clock, I can only delay half an hour. Go and wake up the old master and your old lady, right? Guizhi just held her husband's hand, how could she answer a word? (322)

New Invention

Proof of Kerosene Curing Lung Disease (Middle)

— Bingyu

Kawasaki's workers, once drank fifty grams of it, and there was no harm, but according to the actual experiment, after the first drink, there will probably be diarrhea side effects, and also because the amount is too much, there will also be sore throat and hoarseness. But this phenomenon is temporary, and it will recover immediately after stopping. Especially when diarrhea occurs, according to the experimenters; it can increase appetite and refresh the mind. As for the type of kerosene, any kind can be drunk. It is always better to use second-class oil, too high-quality and gasoline volatile oil (gasoline) must never be taken.

(2) Dr. Iwamoto Yoshitora, Doctor of Science at the Osaka Municipal Industrial Research Institute, proved the effectiveness of kerosene in curing lung diseases. He said: People with insufficient knowledge think that kerosene is poisonous. For more than ten years, in relation to the research on oil, I have long believed that kerosene is the most effective medicine for treating lung diseases. Kerosene is extracted from hundreds of feet underground, and the cause of kerosene has not been determined, but it is believed to be an animal source. We decompose the corpses of fish and other animals that lived in ancient times, eliminating proteins and water-containing carbon, and its fat can be divided into fatty acids and glycerin. Fatty acids are insoluble in water and accumulate in one place, so if they are decomposed again, they will turn into kerosene. If you analyze the salt water of the oil well, the thermal decomposition of fish oil, kerosene contains the same fatty acids as fish oil. Today, kerosene is made from soybean oil and fish oil. I personally separated four and five tenths of a kerosene from one liter of fish oil. This kind of kerosene is also found in the animal and vegetable oils that we eat in our daily diet. Moreover, people in the cold zone in Siberia often drink kerosene. The kerosene punging used in medical treatment is used for disinfection, washing, or scabies and insect repellent. As for internal use, medical books are used as a medicine for abnormal fermentation of the stomach and chronic intestinal catarrh, which is injected into capsules for internal use. (0.3 grams to 0.9 grams per day) We often see kerosene emulsions, which are strong medicines for killing bacteria and insects. This is made by adding an emulsifier to kerosene and stirring. The kerosene becomes very small microparticles, which do not hinder plants and achieve the purpose of killing insects. Thinking this way, kerosene entering the human body is certainly not harmful. Drinking kerosene allows the strong bactericide contained in kerosene to be absorbed into the human body's tissues and circulate throughout the body. Especially when it reaches the affected area in the body, it can exert its bactericidal effect. Furthermore, the food we take in our daily life contains fat and salt. When it reaches the stomach and intestines, due to subtle physiological effects, it forms a soapy state. Because of its strong emulsification, it turns nutrients that are difficult to absorb into emulsions, so that the absorption from the intestinal wall can easily take effect. Therefore, drinking kerosene is not only rich in penetration, but also forms water and emulsions. The kerosene emulsion formed in this way is absorbed from the intestinal tract of the digestive system, enters the blood, and circulates throughout the body. This kerosene, after being used, must be excreted in the urine of the drinker, or seep out from the skin. Judging from this fact, kerosene reaches the lungs, and accompanied by the respiratory function of the lungs, causes the tuberculosis bacteria in the affected area to take effect, so as to eliminate them. I once drank one hundred grams of kerosene continuously, and there was no harm. I also explained in detail the points that I believed to friends who suffered from lung disease, and they also automatically drank it. After that, their results were excellent. However, in order to promote the cause of patients with chronic diseases in society, I often advertise in newspapers and magazines. In the past year, three or four thousand people have directly asked me about the drinking method. Most of these three or four thousand people suffer from lung disease, and most of them are close to the third stage. Because I cannot answer each letter one by one, I specially used a mimeograph to print out the kerosene treatment for lung disease instructions and send them to the questioners. Now, almost all over Japan are drinking it. After they get my instructions, they drink and recover according to the law. It can be said that they are successful. Therefore, letters thanking me fly like mold. A few months ago, a doctor seriously opposed me, saying "Kerosene entering the body of a weak lung disease patient has a hundred harms and no benefits, and it is a violation of the medical profession for people other than doctors to advocate drinking kerosene."

Free Talk

Bat

— Weiming

There used to be such a story: birds and beasts formed groups and fought each other, and there was a kind of bat in between. After the birds won, they flew to the birds, boasting that they had wings and could fly; when the beasts won, they climbed to the beasts, boasting that they could walk, and it was considered a beast. Later, the two realized this, reconciled, and jointly killed the bat. This story can be easily found in elementary school textbooks.

This bat can be considered absurd! At the same time, it is also very funny! It is too lacking. At most, it can only see the direction of the wind and join the victorious group. First: it cannot sing the praises of the victor's merits and expound the reasons why the other party should fail. Second: it cannot think of ways to make the birds and beasts fight forever, so as to obtain many benefits. Third: it cannot be impartial and detached from both, and of course, it can also obtain more benefits.

Humans are the spirit of all things, so their ideas are better than bats. The ancients watched snakes fight and realized the principle of cursive calligraphy, and even learned health preservation from turtles. The so-called Tao follows nature, and humans have learned quite a few methods from the natural world. However, bats are not as good as people, and they really should learn from people: for example, A and B fighting each other can be considered a war; C living in the middle, uniting A to attack B or uniting B to attack A can be considered politics; saying the reason why B or A should be beaten can be considered an ism. So many past facts are history... Reasoning down like this, you will know that "the world is nothing more than that." This is where humans are far superior to animals.

Many of the so-called conspirators in the world are actually "sun" schemes. The art of vertical and horizontal manipulation was popular for a while in ancient times, but it seems to be nothing more than that. Because no matter how you use your wrists and scheming, being in the position of an onlooker but actually being the initiator can be "yin"; but it is inevitable to have an effect, and if there is an effect, there will be facts, and this will all be expressed, inevitably "yang." For example, standing on a scale to measure weight, standing lightly or standing hard is really no different, the weight is the same. Even if the cause and effect are mixed, there is no reversal, and whatever the original shape is, it will eventually be clear. Although Su and Zhang are strategists, no one in ancient and modern times has felt that they have anything other than being strategists. Even if they manage to make the birds and beasts fight forever, they themselves are nothing more than "bats."

Only by thinking this way is there some hope in the world. No matter how dark it is, truth is still truth, and light is still light. Spies have never served as emperors, and hooligans have never become poets. Just look at those people's faces that are so "憔悴深顰," and you can know that there are still "humanity" and "conscience" and the like pressing on them, which is better than the torture in hell.

Snow Pig

— He Yitian

In Xikang, there is an animal, short and no more than two chi long, with light yellow-black fur, resembling a civet, but with a short tail. It walks on its hind legs, while its front legs are held in front of its neck, as if making an arch. It seems to murmur something in its mouth, and people say it is chanting scriptures. It often walks back and forth in the snow, with its tail tucked in and shaking its head. As soon as it sees people, it burrows into a hole. People call it "snow pig." There is a kind of oil inside its belly, white, which can be used to treat frostbite. Perhaps it is because it murmurs in its mouth, it is very peaceful, often making an arch and offering no resistance, being caught from its hole and having its belly cut open with a shiny knife, while it still seems to murmur in its mouth.

This creature is abundant on the west bank of the Jinsha River in Xikang. However, that place is already the territory of Tibetan soldiers led by British officers. In the past, when I was in Batang, I often suffered from frostbite, and hearing that the oil of this animal was very effective, I was always looking for it through people. Once, I met a representative of the thirty-ninth tribe who had his nose cut off by Tibetan soldiers. I thought he would definitely have a solution, but as soon as I mentioned the west bank of the Jinsha River, he shed tears and wiped his eyes. It is said that they are also Han Chinese, who have lived in Tibet for several generations. But as soon as the Tibetan soldiers arrived, they had their noses cut off under the command of British officers, and were forced to flee the Jinsha River. I was afraid he would say more, so I seized an opportunity to ask him if snow pigs were easy to find. But he shook his head at me, seemingly indicating that his family had been destroyed, so how could he talk about snow pigs! He told me that within the Tibetan soldiers' territory, Han people were only allowed to leave, not to enter. When he mentioned this, his face showed an angry expression. Really! His answer was irrelevant! I had no choice but to stand aside, looking from the silver box containing the Buddha statue hanging on his chest to the shallow, festering root of his nose, which was moving slightly. He looked up at the sky, and it seemed that he was murmuring something in his mouth again.

It is said that they had resisted before, perhaps because they were always murmuring in their mouths, they finally peacefully and without resistance allowed the shiny knife to cut off their noses, just like the snow pigs, still murmuring in their mouths.

I am very fortunate, fortunate that I am not on the west bank of the Jinsha River, and not to be cut off my nose; and even more fortunate, thinking that I was born in the mainland that has received the baptism of science, not to be cut off my nose while murmuring in my mouth. Although I am always somewhat apprehensive, I always think that there will be such a day. As soon as I left Xikang, I forgot about it. But now I am worried again: now many people are not playing with prayer beads and murmuring in their mouths again? And recently, many people who think they understand science have also started playing with prayer beads and murmuring in their mouths, and even seem to want to make it a universal trend as if it were a serious matter. During this so-called "national crisis," when foreign command knives are flying everywhere, I am very worried, not afraid of having my nose cut off, but afraid that when being cut, I can only murmur in my mouth.

"There is no greater sorrow than the death of the heart!" I don't know why, I thought of that snow pig walking on the snow, making an arch.

Random Notes on Poetry from Qu Lu

— Chen Zizhan

Xie Maoqin, the "minor poet" of the Ming Dynasty, once said that poetry should avoid vulgar and ugly words, but when used by the right person, adorned with beauty, they can still make for fine lines. It is like a wealthy family's kitchen, where wild vegetables are obtained and seasoned with various flavors, creating a unique taste that is very different from that of a poor family. He also said that the word "blood" is rarely used in poetry, as its use tends to be vulgar and ugly. However, Li Changji's "White Tiger March" says, "Dragon robes stained with Jing Ke's blood." And Gu Buweng's "Song of the Green Bamboo Whip" says, "The fresh green seems dyed with Chang Hong's blood." These two masters are skilled in phrasing, requiring no seasoning; how can wild vegetables have flavor?

I occasionally write poetry, without caring to distinguish the elegance or ugliness of the words, and I also like to use the word "blood." I once sent a seven-character律诗 to Huang Zhigang, which was published in the "Tao Sheng Weekly," with the lines, "Bitter words can be written mixed with blood, smiling faces are rarely seen without a frown." And seven years ago, lamenting the novelist Luo Heizhi, there were also the lines, "I wish to write a hundred thousand words, to carve out my liver and pour out my blood to tell of grievances." Heizhi was once implicated in a certain suspicion and imprisoned for more than a month. Although he was later released after the truth came to light, he ultimately died of grief and indignation. If the minor poet were to see this use of the word "blood," would he still say it is vulgar and ugly, unadorned, like wild vegetables requiring no seasoning?

In the spring of 1928, I and a certain gentleman were working at a certain art academy. He had no tolerance for alcohol but liked to drink yellow wine, and he had no addiction to opium but liked to smoke it. Was he perhaps what is called a heartbroken man with hidden feelings? One day, he said that he was going back to Jiangyin. I thought of Jiangyin as the hometown of Zhou Shuiping, a former professor at Shanghai University. Zhou was killed by Sun Chuanfang, a warlord of the Northern Warlords, for a certain crime, and Wu Zhihui wrote an essay to express his indignation, saying, "Is it feared not to be red, so it is dyed with blood?" This was published in the "Yu Si Weekly." Moved by the times and saddened by events, I wrote a poem to send to the gentleman, and had already drafted it, but a friend saw it and said that the gentleman was returning home to marry a wife, so I destroyed it. The poem reads:

The red land is stained without cause? The birds sing mournfully in spring.

Amidst the bloody wind and rain, I return to mourn Zhou Shuiping in Jiangyin!

If it is said that literature is a tool for venting indignation and proclaiming grief, then in terms of poetry, Qu Yuan, Du Fu, and Wu Meicun should be considered the three greatest writers in our country, and even the poems of Lu You and Yuan Yishan are still considered too weak. With the talent and character of these three masters, they were indeed exceptional, but they happened to live in difficult times, and expressed their poignant words, which is why they are unique throughout the ages. During the reign of Emperor Wuzong of Ming, Zheng Shanfu wrote poetry emulating Du Fu, with many generous and emotional works. Lin Zhenheng, who compiled the Fuzhou Gazetteer, criticized him for not being in the Tianbao era, and for being far from picking up what others left behind, and for groaning without illness. I also have a habit of groaning, but what is the nature of my illness is still waiting to be diagnosed. What I can be sure of is that life is finite, and my strength is very limited, so I am afraid that I cannot seep my blood and tears into the ink, and convey them through my pen!

A Comedy of Tragedy

— Shiheng

("The Triumph of Medicine." A Three-Act Comedy. By Jules Romains of France. Translated by Li Liewen. Published by The Commercial Press.)

I really don't know what to call this kind of work, whether "a comedy of tragedy" or "a tragedy of comedy" is more appropriate?

What I mean is this: we often see many books that are defined as comedies, and on the surface, they do indeed have a bit of a humorous flavor, often providing readers with laughter. But all true art cannot take laughter as its ultimate goal. In the midst of laughter, the author always intentionally or unintentionally hints at a problem, or expresses a reality. From the perspective of the purpose of art, it is no different from tragedy. Many young people or shallow people highly worship tragedy and despise comedy, because they cannot understand the origin of true comedy.

Many comedies often give a dim ending amidst laughter, leaving the reader with a heavier heart than a tragedy. This is true depression, which is different from the effect of tragedy. Tragedy gives a sweet aftertaste in the unfortunate ending of an event; while comedy often shows the true foolishness and evil deeds of human beings from dry reality. It is like a mirror, making a certain kind of person, often many kinds of people, see the ugliness they have always hidden. Therefore, the writing methods of tragedy and comedy are also different. Tragedy goes from poetry to poetry, while comedy goes from prose to poetry; although comedy only has poetic lyricism in the last moment, that power can sometimes surpass everything that tragedy can give. Naturally, due to the different temperaments of people, the views on tragedy and comedy are also different, and I also have no intention of despising tragedy. On the contrary, the comedy that I love to read is precisely because it is not just a comedy, it can be called a "comedy of tragedy." This point needs to be understood. Those comedies that start with laughter and end with laughter, and tell us nothing from laughter, are shallow comedies.

I once translated the Russian great comedian Gogol's "The Story of How the Two Ivans Quarrelled." The content of that story is the most annoying and trivial, but at the end, the author reaches the highest expression of poetry, transforming all the annoying and trivial things into moving ones. In China, there has also been "The True Story of Ah Q," which has a humorous exterior and a painful core. These works do not give you a bit of anesthetizing sweetness after reading, but are more concrete than anything else in representing a certain kind of reality. Recently, I saw "The Triumph of Medicine" by the French writer Jules Romains, and I got the same impression.

According to the translator's introduction, Jules Romains is a playwright who has been working tirelessly in France for the past ten years, and his representative work "The Triumph of Medicine" has achieved rare success on the stage. "When it was first staged, it was performed continuously five hundred times, and the audience did not decrease significantly." Such a result may be excessive, but it has its reasons for success.

Like all comedies, "The Triumph of Medicine" has no content, or in other words, its content cannot be repeated. The translator of this book tells us that: this is "depicting a doctor who does not understand medicine, but understands the psychology of the masses, and how he uses the signboard of science to intimidate the masses and achieve success." This doctor is named Knock. He bought the right to be a doctor in a small town from another doctor. He hired a drummer to promote him. He also persuaded the local elementary school principal to do medical promotion for him. Moreover, he specially created free medical consultations. Everyone who came into his hospital, even those who were not sick, became sick; it would be a bit wrong to say that he was completely intimidating people, because he believed that there were no healthy people in the world, and everyone's body contained microbes, and he certainly believed so. It is absolutely true that he understands the psychology of the masses. Not only does he understand, but he also knows how to be considerate. He knows very well how much wealth a person must have to bear what kind of patient. He determines the severity of your illness according to your ability to pay. His meaning is this, there is no one in the world who is not sick, and it is indeed necessary to diagnose and treat the sick, but if you do not have the ability to pay for medical expenses, then the illness is not very important. But if you are very wealthy, then even if your illness is very mild, he must "intimidate you" to make you fall into bed. According to his investigation, the small town where he practiced medicine has "eight hundred and fifty-three households in the whole town, and among them there are one thousand five hundred and two households whose true annual income is more than twelve thousand francs." Moreover, he "has four levels of treatment. The lowest level is set for those whose annual income is between twelve thousand and twenty thousand francs, allowing only one outpatient visit per week and spending about fifty francs per month on medicine. The highest level, namely luxury treatment, is set for those whose annual income is more than fifty thousand francs, at least teaching them to have four outpatient visits per week and spending three hundred francs per month on miscellaneous expenses, including X-rays, radiation, electrical massage, analysis, general therapy, etc..." (To be continued)

The Diary of Marie Machinaff (II)

— Translated by Ye Zi

This morning 丨丨 From this morning on, my heart has been beating non-stop. A man passed by my window. I saw him coming down from the pasture and walking to the river. Heavens, how handsome he is! He is definitely not as massive as Alexi, no! He is small and strong, as strong as that poor cabbage yesterday.

He was wearing a velvet veston, carrying a folding stool and easel, a cigarette holder, and a smile that lit up his face, just like moonlight shining on a milky white bowl.

Am I in love with him? ...I don't know... When he passed by my window, I threw a rose ball at him... but he didn't notice. So I threw soap and a toothbrush at him again... but I missed again, he just went his way.

X X X X X X X X

Another day 丨丨 Love has broken into my life... I saw him again! I even spoke to him! He was sitting on his little stool. He was painting. I asked his name. His name! ...Thinking of writing this name, my heart jumped again. No... I won't write it out, I'll just say it softly: it's Odo Dinkesbeer.

What a beautiful name!

I also asked him:

"What are you painting at this moment? Is it the baby Jesus?"

"No," he said to me, "I'm painting a cow."

I looked closely. It was indeed a cow. So I shot my gaze into his pupils and said:

"This is our secret. We must not reveal it to anyone."

X X X X X X X X

A week later 丨丨 Every morning, I always go to the pasture to see Odo. I sit beside him and tell him in detail what I think, what I read, what I know, what I feel, and everything I don't feel. He listens with an attitude that seems not to be listening, which makes me fascinated. The closeness of our souls is wonderful.

X X X X X X X X

Today 丨丨 Odo touched me... This memory still makes my heart palpitate. By the river, when I was standing next to him, the edge of my parasol touched the last button on his vest... I suddenly felt a burning fire... Tomorrow, I will take Odo to see my dad.

X X X X X X X X

The next day 丨丨 Odo beat my dad. He hit my dad with ten rubles. Dad was furious. He forbade Odo's foot from stepping on the floor of my house again. From now on, Odo and I can only meet by the river.

X X X X X X X X

Foreign Exchange Still Has No Price

No White Borrowing Since Market Opening

Yesterday, the market price of foreign exchange continued to be "white borrowing". The premium rate in the Small Exchange Association was only two or three cents, also a "white premium". The looseness and excessiveness of the market atmosphere were unparalleled. The turnover of exchange bills in the early market increased compared to the previous day, reaching over 2.7 million. New transactions amounted to over 500,000, and transactions in the Small Exchange Association exceeded 200,000. Although yesterday was Monday, bank settlements were not very busy. Foreign banks settled over 1.5 million in bills and notes, over 3.3 million in various goods, foreign exchange collateral, and miscellaneous items, over 800,000 in closing accounts, and 400,000 in warehouse entries. Chinese banks settled over 2.4 million in bills and notes, over 4 million in various goods, tax collateral, and miscellaneous items, over 1.4 million in closing accounts, and 300,000 in warehouse exits. Japanese banks settled over 2 million in bills and notes, over 2.45 million in various miscellaneous items, and 400,000 in warehouse exits. Money shops settled over 25 million in foreign public bills, over 3.45 million in foreign premium accounts, over 400,000 in various remittance accounts, and 200,000 to 300,000 in cash. Foreign collateral transactions amounted to over 400,000. In terms of banknote inflow and outflow, approximately 500,000 was recovered, and over 700,000 was issued. Sources from various routes amounted to 200,000, and outflows amounted to 150,000. Furthermore, the total exchange volume at the clearing house was 30,045,448.72 silver dollars, including 7,131,254.46 silver dollars in cash and 23,323,294.26 silver dollars in remittances.

Among Subsidiary Currencies, Only Jiangnan Coins Rose

Yesterday, Jiangnan small silver coins rose by five yuan in the early market compared to the previous day, reaching 850 yuan, with 2,500 coins transacted. There was no market at noon as usual. Guangdong small silver coins remained unchanged in the early market, with the same price as the previous day at 770 yuan, with 60,000 coins transacted. Copper coins remained unchanged at 319,000 cash, with 11,400 yuan transacted, totaling 36,366 strings of cash. All prices were halted at noon.

Grand Occasion of Public Bond Delivery in February Securities Market

丨Total Transaction Volume of 61.04 Million Yuan丨

丨Exchange Delivery of 19.14 Million Yuan丨

丨Self-Delivery of 41.9 Million Yuan丨

New High Prices Emerge One After Another

All Items Break Old Records

Yesterday, February 26th, was the delivery date for the February futures of public bonds at the Chinese Securities Exchange. The settlement volume on this day was extremely large, an unprecedented grand occasion in recent times. The total amount reached a huge 61.04 million yuan. Among this, excluding the clearing of accounts by various brokers, the amount for self-delivery was 41.9 million yuan. The amount for actual delivery at the exchange was 19.14 million yuan. The account settlement by various brokers outside the exchange was not included. Although the number cannot be verified, it must also be very large. The settlement volume is truly remarkable. The five-number bond was the most received. Other groups also had scattered absorption. The financial sector accounted for the most delivered. The market price trend is also worth mentioning. The February futures debuted on December 30th of the previous year and ended on February 22nd. Although it lasted for more than fifty days, due to the Lunar New Year and the abolition of the old lunar year with more than ten days of holidays, there were actually only more than forty market days. When the February futures debuted, it coincided with the autumn of the Min Incident. Therefore, it was immediately affected after the opening. Later, the central army successively won victories, conquering Taishun. The 19th Route Army abandoned Yanping, Gutian was captured, and Fuzhou was occupied in a few days. With the Min Incident resolved, people's confidence became even stronger. The buying sentiment was extremely strong, and the bond market continued to rise. New high prices emerged one after another. After the red opening of the abolished Lunar New Year, the upward trend intensified. Later, due to the recent loose monetary conditions and white borrowing of silver exchange every day, investors increased, and the bond market rose even more vigorously. When the futures trading was suspended on the 22nd, the Deficit Reduction Bond still rushed to the 70 yuan mark, creating a new high price of 70 yuan and 1.5 cents, breaking the record of 69 yuan and 2 cents on July 19th of the 22nd year. The Salt Tax Bond also rose to 53 yuan and 3 cents. Other items also broke the old year's records. After the February suspension of trading, due to the high prices, some floating long positions emerged, and sellers began to divest. In addition, rumors spread in the market, and the lively market was slightly sluggish. However, many people still held optimistic views, and the bond market may not decline as a result. Grain: Flour Factories Eager to Sell

丨Government Bids U.S. Wheat at Four Yuan

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, all months showed a consistent decline. U.S. wheat quotations were slightly better by 4 cents in Chicago and 2 cents in Canada, with little fluctuation. Therefore, after the opening price, the market atmosphere was still stable. However, various factories sold off, and sales gradually became very active. Several large factories, with a large number of hedged goods on hand, sold in large quantities. In addition, the selling price of spot U.S. wheat also gradually declined. The government seemed eager to sell, with a price of only 4 yuan. However, factories were still unwilling to buy. Therefore, each month continued to decline. Until the afternoon opening, the bulls inside and outside the industry felt that it was useless to resist in such an environment, so they also closed out one after another. Furthermore, with the selling by factories, the selling sentiment in the market became even more active, and prices became even weaker. According to speculation by people in the industry, if the government wheat is sold cheaply without end, the two-yuan mark may be within sight. As a result, the current month fell by 3.75 cents compared to the previous week, March fell by 2.5 cents, April and May fell by 3 cents, June fell by 2.5 cents, and July fell by 2.25 cents.

Futures Wheat Sales Not Yet Rushing Out

Yesterday, after the futures wheat market opened in the morning and afternoon, the market situation for each month was generally flat and weak. U.S. wheat quotations were better by 4 cents in Chicago and about 2 cents in Canada. The market sentiment remained flat and weak. Soon, with the flour market weakening and the government wheat gradually becoming loose, it seemed that there was no possibility of optimism for future prices. However, market sales were not very active. Therefore, although the situation for each month was not good, the extent of the decline was small. As a result, April fell by 5 cents compared to the previous week, June fell by 5 cents, and July fell by 3 cents. There were no comparisons for the rest. The spot wheat market price was stable. It was reported that kiln bay wheat was 3.43 yuan, Suzhou wheat was 3.42 yuan, Huangqiao wheat was 3.41 yuan, Guzhen wheat was 3.36 yuan, Bengbu wheat was 3.34 yuan, and Kunshan wheat was 3.30 yuan. Fuxin took more than 300 bags, Fufeng took 2,400 bags, and Huafeng took 300 bags.

Northern and Southern Groups Handling Du Rice

Late Rice Arrives in Volume, Falling Several Cents

(South Shanghai) Sources from various groups surged, totaling more than sixty (more than 8,000 stones). Zhongyi and Xi Nong were the most common, while Geng and various colors accounted for half. Since customers from Tianjin and other places seemed interested in buying late rice, now customers from various groups are successively entering the market. Southern Ocean group, Xiamen customers, took the lead in handling, and Tianjin and other groups followed suit, making the situation relatively lively. However, since customers' buying prices were low, sellers had no choice but to sell with pain. As a result, the Northern and Southern Ocean groups purchased more than 2,000 bags. The goods were all green corner, Song Si, Xi Lian, and other goods. The market price fell slightly by a few cents. The local shop business was still sluggish, and sales were still depressed. The market situation was soft and depreciating. Geng rice from Changbang, Su Tongbang, and Nangang continued to be cut by several cents. Du Yangjian rice, due to the shortage of goods, stood firm. The Yin Yuan suddenly became tight, and the Bian Yuan had no honor or disgrace.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, there were more than fifty sources from various groups in Hexia. The sales of various goods in the market improved. The price of Bai Geng, Du Jian, Bu Jian, and early rice was flat and weak. Yang Xian was high and strong. Medium and lower grades were cut by several cents. Bai Yuan and Yin Yuan Keqian were stable.

Sugar Market: Longjiang Green Goods Scarce, Looking to Rise

Yesterday, the Sugar Market Association's pricing showed that although No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar was still quoted at 19.7 yuan, inquiries were still few. The lower-grade Longjiangqing Shandi has been sold out. It is heard that the Suiyang Hesheng two rounds will transport more than a thousand bags today. Because the prices in the production area are firm, the Shanghai market is looking to rise (The previously reported Weijiangqing price of 13.5 yuan was actually 10.05 yuan, please correct).

Based on the market trend, there may be an increase.

丨Still Needs to Watch for Declines丨

Shrimp rice Jinshanwei, because the sales of various routes are not moving, and the arrival inventory is prosperous, the market price of large-sized goods is 105 yuan, medium-sized goods are around 100 yuan, and small-sized goods are 93-94 yuan, which has fallen by 2-3 yuan compared to the red market.
