Piece Goods: Yuanzhi Tribute Substandard Goods Sell Well

丨Slight Changes in the Woolen Industry

Not many new Yuanqing tribute woolen goods have arrived in port. The sales of lower-grade goods are the most fluent. Yesterday, Ning Feng Hang's ten boxes of single-sided tribute were purchased by Hua Fu Tai at a transaction price of 4 yuan net. The goods arrived and were offered for sale at 4.3 yuan. These single-sided tribute and 5.0 yuan substandard double-sided tribute are out of stock, with a considerable risk of being out of stock. Because the exchange rate is slightly better, foreign firms' pricing is 2-3 cents more expensive, so no one orders.

There is news of changes in the woolen industry. It is heard that Yifeng and Huakang's share increases remain the same. Jiuhe and Jiuda are merging into Jiufeng. Jiufeng, Yukang, Xinchang, and Meilun are planning to move to the west side of the fabric exchange next door. Huachengxiang's share increase will change the brand name to Hongxiang. Huasheng and Tonghexiang are changing their font size. Xiangxing's liquidation has been confirmed (Another number is also heard to be liquidated). Fuxin will temporarily move opposite Huaxin and wait for the new house on the original site to be completed before moving in again.

Oil Market: White Tung Oil Spring Market Continues to Fall

White Tung oil trading in Hankou foreign firms is very rare. When the spring market first opened, each foreign firm handled only dozens of tons to a hundred tons, with prices increased to 24.6 yuan per dan according to foreign regulations. Then, Hankou Hang wanted to increase to 25 yuan. The foreign firms' intentions weakened as a result. They held on for three or four days, and still sold about a hundred tons at 24.5-24.6 yuan. Hankou Hang opened the guest goods for 19.23 yuan for the Southern Branch and 19.45 yuan for Changde goods, approximately 2,000-3,000 dan. The closing price in the Hankou market was not much different from the opening price. Although there was a tight period, there were no transactions, only one kind of situation. As for Zhejiang Tung, it was quite powerful because the opening was decorated with Hankou market rumors. But it was just a fleeting moment and the romance dispersed. Therefore, the initial price was 21.7-21.8 yuan for delivery to Shanghai, but it soon fell to 21.2 yuan and 21.07-21.08 yuan, and there was a tendency to fall further. Hangzhou Hang has been sending people to Shanghai to sell for days, but there are not many transactions. Last night, the local firms received a call from Lanxi that it had fallen to 19.6 yuan, with Hangzhou Jianggan delivery, then it would only be 20.02-20.03 yuan to Shanghai. Because each firm has slight winter deposits, there have not been many purchases since the spring market. Only a certain bean and rice firm also deals in foreign Tung oil. It went to Zhejiang last week to complete more than 3,000 dan at a price between 20.07-20.08 yuan. The goods have not yet arrived, and the market has already fallen. Based on the current market, the loss is not insignificant.

Chinese Tallow Market Will Look Small

The Chinese tallow market in this port, since the opening of the spring market, the sales field seems to be clearer than in previous years. Since the spring market is usually slightly higher than the formal market price, only a few people handle it. After the closing, the market situation will inevitably stagnate, and there must be a basis after the markets from everywhere converge. Shanghai originally relied on the Hankou market, and the Hankou market opening is not certain sooner or later. However, it has advanced slightly in recent years, probably determined by the amount of borrowing and loading before the opening. According to this year's borrowing and loading statistics, the unified Hankou market has only a thousand pieces, and the sales clarity is unprecedented. Therefore, the Tianjin market oil futures were opened the day before yesterday, and the price was around 16 yuan. Although the Jing oil has not opened, the general situation is not as powerful as the closing time. It can be generally seen. The firms in this port do not borrow too much from Hankou, and the winter stock is not very thick. In addition, they received the news that the Hankou market opened weak. Therefore, although the sales disk does not show a price drop, the market air has been sluggish, and the secret selling price has not been unified, which seems to be in a shaky state.

Silk and Tea: Gray Silk Has Discovered New Sales Channels

Gray silk from Shandong and other provinces (that is, wild silkworm silk) is a unique natural product in our country and is widely sold in European and American countries. Recently, it has been affected by the dumping of gray silk from Japan and South Korea (Japan and Korea have seen increasing wild silkworm silk production in recent years) and artificial silk, which has caused our country's gray silk exports to plummet. Export has become the end of the crossbow. Recently, India has suddenly discovered a new sales channel. English ships transport dozens of packages to India every month. Therefore, English and Indian firms often purchase gray silk, and the market price has risen by more than 20 yuan compared to the past.

Hardware: Thin Tinplate Market Inventory Is Thin

The spot thin tinplate market was very thin yesterday. Customer groups such as Hankou and Tianjin are vying to seek it, and the tobacco factories, can factories, printing factories, and biscuit factories on this street are also trying their best to find it. Therefore, there are fewer and fewer bottom goods, and the market is becoming more exquisite. What's more, the arrival of goods is far away, so the market atmosphere is becoming more and more upright. The standards have repeatedly increased, calculated at 60 yuan per box, which is 4-5 yuan higher than before. It is heard that more than 70-80 boxes were opened in the market yesterday.

Educational News

Overseas Naval Academy Students First Study Shipbuilding at School

(Nanjing, 26th) The Navy previously agreed with Italy on the method for naval academy students to study abroad. Chen Shaokuan specially hired Ye Yunchiao, who had just returned from the United States and is currently a staff member of the Jiangnan Shipbuilding Institute, to teach shipbuilding at the academy, so that the students can prepare and study in the country first, and then go to Italy to study abroad for further education.

Status of Secondary and Higher Education in Various Counties of Jiangxi

(Nanchang Correspondence) The number of secondary and higher education schools in various counties of Jiangxi Province in the 20th year was 68, with 491 classes, 15,063 students, 1,871 faculty and staff, and an expenditure of 18,710,400 yuan. The number of students per class was 30, and the annual cost per student was 124.124 yuan. In the 21st year, there were 69 schools, 471 classes, 13,663 students, 1,731 faculty and staff, and an expenditure of 17,033,390 yuan. The number of students per class was 29, and the annual cost per student was 124.670 yuan. From the above table, in the 21st year, the number of schools increased by 1, the number of classes decreased by 20, the number of students decreased by 1,400, the number of faculty and staff decreased by 140, and the expenditure decreased by 1,677,010.01 yuan. On the surface, it seems that there is no progress in secondary and higher education, and even a decline. However, the decrease in the number of classes is not a decline, but a reorganization of secondary education, reducing the number of ordinary middle schools and increasing or reorganizing vocational and normal schools. The decrease in the number of students is actually affected by the sharp reduction in the number of joint county, municipal, private, and specialized schools. The number of provincial students has even slightly increased. Because the number of schools has decreased, the annual cost per student has increased compared to the past. In short, the increase in the annual cost per student and the decrease in the number of students in this province cannot but make people suspect that it is difficult to meet the conditions of economy and education. This is a unique phenomenon in Jiangxi Province, so it is necessary to make secondary education, A. In the future, attention should be paid to the administrative aspects: (1) Enrich the content and increase equipment as much as possible; (2) If it is not possible to recruit enough students, only combine classes, etc.

Ministry of Education Releases Statistics on National Colleges and Above

School Funding

The Ministry of Education has compiled statistics on the funding of colleges and above across the country: (1) Annual Revenue Funding (divided into national and provincial treasury funds, property income, donations, student fees, miscellaneous income). The national total is 34,025,786 yuan, (including (1) over 13,478,000 yuan for national universities, over 251,000 yuan for independent colleges, and over 188,000 yuan for specialized schools; (2) over 3,438,000 yuan for provincial universities, over 1,148,000 yuan for independent colleges, and over 867,000 yuan for specialized schools; (3) over 409,000 yuan for public specialized schools; (4) over 7,706,000 yuan for private universities, over 5,873,000 yuan for independent colleges, and over 661,000 yuan for specialized schools;) (2) Annual Expenditure Funding The national total is 33,619,237 yuan, of which 12,142,013 yuan is for teachers' salaries (including 5,342,340 yuan for national universities, independent colleges, and specialized schools, 2,205,633 yuan for provincial universities, independent colleges, and specialized schools, 140,178 yuan for public specialized schools, and 4,453,862 yuan for private universities, independent colleges, and specialized schools), 4,699,917 yuan for staff salaries (1,598,981 yuan for national school staff salaries, 912,429 yuan for provincial school staff salaries, 103,926 yuan for public school staff salaries, and 2,048,578 yuan for private school staff salaries), 1,106,395 yuan for worker wages, 4,056,108 yuan for office expenses, 6,379,778 yuan for equipment expenses, 2,566,235 yuan for special expenses, and 1,412,232 yuan for affiliated institutions.

Local News

Key Points for School Inspectors and Education Committee Members' Inspection of County Education Bureau

The Shanghai County Education Bureau has separately formulated the key points for school inspectors' and education committee members' inspection for this semester and has issued instructions for all schools to comply. The details are as follows: (A) Administration: (1) The National Salvation Program promulgated by the Ministry shall be implemented practically; (2) The key points for improving primary schools promulgated by the Ministry shall be followed for improvement; (3) School affairs shall be properly divided and managed; (4) Various meetings shall be held regularly and legally, and the resolutions shall be effectively implemented; (5) Prescribed forms and registers shall be completed in full, and those with deadlines shall be prepared on schedule; (6) Teachers' qualifications shall meet the regulations; (7) The bureau's calendar of events shall be strictly followed; (8) School affairs shall be carried out with a concrete plan; (9) Finances shall be transparent, and all expenditures shall be accounted for; (10) The curriculum shall meet the standards; (11) The timetable shall be appropriately arranged; (12) The class structure shall be appropriate; (13) Each grade shall have the required number of students, and the average daily attendance rate shall reach 80% or more; (14) School buildings and equipment shall be used economically; (15) The environment shall be arranged with appropriate changes and contain educational and artistic meaning; (16) Sports fields, small libraries, small farms, school gardens, and other facilities shall be properly planned and managed; (17) Attention shall be paid to the air and light in the classrooms, and circulation and absorption shall be ensured; (18) Forms and reports shall be filled out truthfully, and entrusted tasks shall be reported and completed on schedule; (19) Toilets, spittoons, and other facilities shall be inspected regularly and kept clean; (20) The Ministry's methods for contacting families shall be followed; (21) Remedial measures shall be taken for absent students; (22) Newly added school equipment and books shall be registered promptly; (23) The Ministry's methods for primary school teachers' further education shall be diligently followed; (B) Training: (1) Civic training shall be implemented in phases; (2) Civic training shall have concrete assessment methods; (3) Our country's inherent morality shall be promoted as much as possible; (4) Children's good habits shall be cultivated, and bad habits shall be eliminated; (5) Morning exercises and cleanliness inspections shall be implemented; (6) Children's self-government organizations shall be sound; (7) Students' diligent work habits shall be cultivated; (8) Extracurricular activities shall be carefully guided; (9) Physical examinations shall be conducted; (10) Thrift shall be promoted; (11) Extracurricular supervision shall be implemented; (12) Children's individual characteristics shall be assessed and recorded; (C) Teaching: (1) The teaching hours for each subject shall meet the standards; (2) Teaching plans shall be prepared for each subject; (3) Detailed records shall be kept of the implementation of teaching; (4) Report cards for each subject shall be recorded on schedule; (5) Specimens and models shall be collected and made as much as possible; (6) Teaching aids shall be made by oneself; (7) Senior grades shall write compositions weekly, middle grades three times a week, and junior grades twice a week, which shall be strictly followed; (8) Large and small regular script shall be practiced daily, and attention shall be paid to neatness; (9) Each subject shall have notes, and the content shall be enriched; (10) Arithmetic shall be practiced in notebooks three times a week (at least 50 times this semester); (11) There shall be daily and weekly records, with comments added; (12) Each unit of art shall have a representative work, and the grades shall be preserved; (13) Music shall select and teach songs that promote the national spirit and utilize our country's inherent musical instruments; (14) Manual labor teaching shall enable children to engage in practical work; (15) Our country's inherent games shall be promoted.

Board Meeting of the Science Society of China

Appointing Personnel to Review Academic Cases

And Passing Fourteen Regular Members

The Science Society of China held its 116th board meeting the other day. Attendees included Wang Jiliang, Hu Gangfu, Zhao Yuanren, Ren Shuyong, Zhou Zijing, and Yang Yunzhong (represented by Lu Xiune). Ren Shuyong chaired the meeting, and Lu Jine recorded the minutes. The agenda was as follows: (1) There were a total of four papers for the Miss Gao Memorial Award for the 21st year: (1) Wang Dazhu's "Research on Earthquakes," (2) Wang Yijin's "Historical View of Soil," (3) Ding's "Principles of Earthquake Comparison," and (4) Chen Guoda's "Problems of the Pearl River Delta in Guangzhou." The review committee, consisting of Zhu Oufang, Zhang Xiaofeng, and Li Zhongkui, completed the review. According to the opinions of the committee members, Chen Guoda's paper seemed to be the most suitable. Whether it is appropriate or not, please vote. The motion was passed according to the opinion of the review committee, and Chen Guoda's "Problems of the Pearl River Delta in Guangzhou" was selected as the Miss Gao Memorial Award paper for the 21st year. Could the remaining three papers be selected for publication in the Science Journal? Please have Zhu Oufang review them. (2) The funds raised by the Institute of Biology are still far from the quota. The board of directors of the previous session resolved to wait for President Ren to go south to discuss the progress methods. Please resolve the fundraising methods. The motion was passed to postpone the decision on the fundraising methods for the Institute of Biology and proceed with it at any time. (3) For academic cases entrusted to the Society by the outside world for review or to seek the Society's opinions, please decide on the methods. The motion was passed that the General Secretary will invite members of the Society's astronomy and mathematics groups to study the naming and segmentation of arithmetic matters, and the draft of arithmetic terms will be reviewed by the original drafter and Gu Yangwu. (4) The Society was born on June 10, 1914, and formally established on October 25 of the following year. June 10 of this year is the 20th anniversary of its birth. Is it necessary to have a commemorative expression, or wait until October 25 of next year to hold a commemoration? The motion was passed that October 25 of next year will be the 20th anniversary of the establishment of the Society. (5) Society member Ma Minghai, representing Guangxi, invited the Society to hold its annual meeting in Guangxi this summer. The motion was passed that the location of this year's annual meeting was decided at the 18th annual meeting to be in Lushan, and it seems inconvenient to change it now. (6) Fourteen regular members were approved as follows: Feng Zefang (Agronomy), Zhu Jixun (Biology), Pan Zhuqi (Agronomy), Liu Zengmian (Engineering), Hu Mingshi (Civil Engineering), Fan Huiguo (Mathematics and Physics), Wang Zongling (Science), Wang Guoyuan (History), Zhang Defu (Education), Wang Jigang (Mechanical Aviation), Xiao Shufeng (Medicine), Tu Jicheng (Physics and Chemistry), Xiong Chungao (Mechanical), Chen Huaqing (Dentistry), Associate Member Huang Lüping (Wireless Electricity). (7) Guangxi member Ma Xinyi sent a letter proposing to establish a Society Friendship Association in Wuzhou, and has contacted Team Minghai, the Dean of the College of Science of Guangxi University, and has received his agreement. The Society has now sent the Society charter to facilitate the process. The meeting was adjourned.

The Chinese Western Academy of Sciences Sends Personnel to Inspect Agricultural Affairs in Various Places

Inspector Liu Shimin Arrived in Shanghai from Hangzhou Yesterday

There Is Great Hope for the Revival of Agriculture in Sichuan Province

The Chinese Western Academy of Sciences in Beipei, Chongqing, Sichuan, is a large-scale scientific research institution in our country. Although it has only been established for two years, its achievements are remarkable. Everyone who goes to Sichuan and Xikang praises the academy. The academy recently sent Liu Shimin, the director of the botanical garden and a researcher at the botanical department, to inspect agricultural affairs in various places and visit scientific research institutions. Liu visited Yantai, Laiyang, Peiping, Tianjin, Baoding, Dingxian, Ningbo, Hangzhou, and other places, and arrived in Shanghai from Hangzhou yesterday, staying at the Mengyuan Hostel. He is scheduled to visit the Commodity Inspection Bureau, Serum Manufacturing Institute, and other institutions within the next few days, and will return to Sichuan in a few days. Yesterday, a Shanghai News reporter visited Liu at the hostel to discuss the establishment process and recent work as follows:

Establishment Process

The academy has been established for two years so far. The president is Mr. Lu Zuoji. The sources of funding include fixed subsidies from the 21st Army and the China Cultural Foundation Committee, and non-fixed subsidies from the Sichuan Education Expenditure Office, Minsheng Shipping Company, and Sichuan-Kang Colonial Bank, as well as funds from other research institutions for entrusted projects. The total annual amount is approximately 60,000 to 100,000 yuan. The salaries of the staff are not high, but they are quite willing to sacrifice, and their spirit of service is commendable.

Internal Organization

The academy's internal structure is divided into four parts: the Institute of Physics and Chemistry, the Institute of Geology, the Institute of Biology, and the Institute of Agriculture and Forestry. The Institute of Physics and Chemistry is cooperating with the Institute of Physics and Chemistry of the Academia Sinica. The Institute of Geology is cooperating with the Geological Survey of Peiping of the Academia Sinica. The Institute of Biology is cooperating with the Jing Sheng Biological Investigation Institute and the Science Society of China. The Institute of Agriculture and Forestry is currently negotiating cooperation with the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry of the China Economic Commission.

Recent Work

The academy's Department of Physics and Chemistry is currently analyzing mineral products from various places near Beipei, the Department of Geology is investigating the geology of the Jialing River, the Department of Agriculture and Forestry is implementing rice breeding, pest control, and special fruit tree propagation experiments, and is carrying out afforestation in various wastelands in Beipei. More than 8,000 kinds of special fruit seedlings were collected by Liu this time. The Department of Biology is carrying out preliminary research work, collecting and classifying all Sichuan flora and fauna, and establishing a botanical garden, gathering Sichuan plants in one garden, so that people from other places who come to Sichuan for visits do not have to travel to various places. The garden is currently being measured and construction is underway.

Agricultural Experiments

Chen Rangqing, the director of the Sichuan Central Agricultural Experiment Station, also came to Shanghai. According to him, the station is the only large-scale experiment station in Sichuan Province, funded and organized by the Sichuan Post-War Rehabilitation Office (i.e., Liu Xiang of the 21st Army), established for one and a half years, and is a provincial agricultural station. It is divided into four departments: agronomy, horticulture, animal husbandry, and agricultural chemistry. The agronomy department focuses on cotton planting experiments, and its cotton planting results have exceeded those of the southeastern provinces. The horticulture department focuses on the improvement, storage, and transportation of citrus fruits, as the surrounding counties are citrus-producing areas. The animal husbandry department focuses on pigs and sheep, and the agricultural chemistry department specializes in agricultural product manufacturing. According to Liu, Sichuan Province has abundant resources and is of great importance to national defense. The products of both southern and northern China are suitable for cultivation in Sichuan. The degree of agricultural improvement has already shown signs of revival. If efforts continue, the future of Sichuan Province is promising.

The Municipal Education Bureau Sends Personnel to Conduct Maze Intelligence Tests in Suzhou and Wuxi

Intelligence testing of children is of great importance to the improvement of primary school administration. The resolution of all issues related to admission grading and teaching research must rely on the assistance of intelligence testing in order to have objective results. However, the results of intelligence tests compiled in our country in the past have not been significant. The Pinay-Simon test materials compiled and printed by the Chinese Education Improvement Society seven years ago were not fully suitable for kindergarten and lower grades of primary schools, perhaps due to the slightly higher cost and complicated procedures. In view of this, the Municipal Education Bureau has adopted the Porteus Maze Test scale to create a simple and effective intelligence test scale to supplement the deficiencies of the Pinay-Simon test scale. Last year, the bureau tested approximately 4,000 children in this city and the cities of Nanjing and Hangzhou. Currently, the number of children of each age tested is uneven, which hinders statistics. It is planned to conduct tests in other cities to increase the number to 6,000. It is reported that the bureau has decided to send personnel to primary schools in Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, Zhenjiang, and other places in early next month to conduct the intelligence tests, so that children from different social environments in various places can be tested together, and the results may be more accurate and universally applicable.

City Education Bureau Orders Students with Dental Problems to Go to the Children's Dental Hospital

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to all primary and secondary schools in the city, stating: "Based on a report from the Family Industries Society, 'In order to promote dental health and oral hygiene, and for the sake of the healthy well-being of children, our society has established the Children's Dental Hospital at No. 191-193, 2nd Floor, Nanjing Road, Shanghai, in a central location. The scope of diagnosis and treatment is limited to boys and girls under the age of sixteen. Those over sixteen will not be accepted under any circumstances. However, students in primary and secondary schools in this city, even if they are over the age of sixteen, who have a dental treatment form issued by the Municipal Education Bureau, are exempt from this restriction. Please instruct all schools that any student with unhealthy teeth should be referred to the hospital for examination to avoid hindering the child's development. Our society will charge diagnosis fees according to regulations to fulfill its social service responsibilities.' Based on this, it is recognized that children's teeth are of great importance to their health. If students in your school have dental defects, they should seek treatment immediately. In addition to the children's dental clinics established by the Health Bureau and this bureau, schools can also go to the Children's Dental Hospital for treatment. However, students over the age of sixteen must first obtain an introduction form from this bureau before going for examination. You are hereby ordered to take note of this order."

First Act of the Sino-British Billiards Competition: Li Gongying Wins a Great Victory

Defeats Botter by 424 Points Yesterday

Unlimited Hope for the Future of the Chinese Team

The second Sino-British International Billiards Competition began yesterday afternoon at 5:30 PM at the Shanghai Amateur Billiards Club. The Chinese team's star player, Li Gongying, started off by defeating the British player Botter by a large margin, winning by 424 points out of a total of 750 points, giving unlimited hope for the future of the Chinese team. Tomorrow afternoon at 5:30 PM, Shen Lince will face Nie Kerer, promising a fierce battle.

A General View of the Art

Li's victory over Botter was never in question. What was noteworthy was how Li was able to display his own aspirations. Fifty shots for 750 points, averaging 15 points per shot, can be considered an excellent score in Li's previous records of competition with major strong opponents. Yesterday's largest scores were 93, 74, 68, 65, 58, 53, 52, etc. It is regrettable that the last few shots showed some weakness; otherwise, the average score could have been close to 20. The British Botter, a white-haired veteran, was relaxed in his attitude. He was still able to cope with a cue in his hand. He used the "open teng" several times, with much of the Smith style. Limited by his qualifications, he was defeated after exhausting his strength. His large scores were 42, 39, 37, 29, 20, etc., averaging slightly more than 6.5 points per shot, which seemed to be slightly less than usual.

Competition Situation

Li scored 16 points on the first shot, and Botter also scored 16 points on the second shot. After three missed shots, Li scored two huge scores of 58 and 33 in a row, taking the lead. Botter scored 39 points on the seventh shot, followed by 20 points, bringing the score closer. Li scored an unexpectedly lucky ball, scoring 52 points in a row, once imitating Smith's tactics and scoring 65 points. Once, when the opponent's ball had already entered the pocket, he also scored 74 points by hitting a red ball alone. The largest score of 93 points was obtained due to various methods, which was extremely interesting. Before the 50th shot was finished, he had already scored 44 points, ending the game. Botter was 77 points behind on the 10th shot, 120 points behind between the 10th and 20th shots, and only 54 points behind between the 20th and 30th shots. In the last 20 shots, however, the difference was quite large. As a result, he lost by a total of 424 points.

Municipal Sports Field Organizes Amateur Basketball Association

Will Continue to Organize a Table Tennis Association in the Future

The Municipal Sports Field organizes an amateur basketball competition every spring, holding outdoor basketball games with remarkable results. This spring, it will continue to organize the fourth amateur basketball competition, starting registration on March 3 and closing on March 25. The players of the participating teams must be purely amateur members of the industrial and commercial sectors. School students and those who take sports as a profession are not allowed to participate. At the time of registration, a registration form printed by the association must be filled in detail and a photo of all team members must be attached. The competition dates are on Saturday afternoons and all day on Sundays, which does not interfere with the professions of various sectors. The association has printed a detailed set of regulations for those who wish to participate, which can be requested and read. In addition, the field has recently set up seven table tennis rooms in the south building, in order to popularize practice. After the basketball competition is over, it is planned to hold a table tennis competition immediately to promote indoor sports.

Minutes of the Preparatory Standing Committee of the National Martial Arts Unification Committee

The first meeting of the Standing Committee of the Preparatory Committee of the National Martial Arts Unification Committee was held at 3:00 PM on February 21 in the conference hall of the Central Martial Arts Museum. Those present were Hao Gengsheng, Chu Minyi, Wu Tunan, Liu Shenzhen, Zhang Zhijiang, Jiang Rongqiao, and Cheng Dengke. Those attending as observers were Wu Junshan and Jin Yiming. Zhang Zhijiang served as the chairman, and Jin Yiming served as the recorder. The ceremony was conducted as scheduled. Regarding the reporting of matters, the drafting committee reported that the declaration of the preparatory committee, the organizational outline, and the rules and regulations of the unification committee's proceedings have all been drafted and still need to be sorted out. They will be distributed to the committees for review. Matters for discussion included: (1) proposing whether other important preparatory committee members can be invited to attend future standing committee meetings in order to gather ideas and contribute opinions. It should be decided by public vote. Decision: Future standing committee meetings will inform preparatory committee members to participate. (2) proposing whether to appoint a drafter to prepare a martial arts implementation plan. Please decide by public vote. Decision: The committee will first do the basic work and first start with the outline organization, then organize separately. The drafting of the implementation plan will be temporarily reserved. After the various declarations and regulations are announced, the drafting committee will be appointed. (3) proposing that before the Unification Committee is formally established, can the committee, in its name, send letters to the national provincial, municipal, and county martial arts museums and other martial arts societies, martial arts associations, and martial arts organizations to investigate the names and categories of the boxing techniques and weapons taught by those organizations for reference. Please decide by public vote. Decision: The committee tasked Hao Gengsheng, Cheng Dengke, and Wu Tunan to draft a survey form and then print and distribute it. (4) proposing whether the official seal of the Standing Committee of the Unification Committee's Preparatory Committee should be discussed and decided separately for use. Please decide by public vote. Decision: The style was decided, and the committee tasked Jiang Rongqiao with taking responsibility for handling it. (5) proposing when is the appropriate date to convene a general assembly of the Unification Committee. Please decide by public vote. Decision: The date of the general assembly will be decided when the preparation is mature and necessary. (6) proposing whether the number of members of the Unification Committee has been determined, and whether the candidates for each committee should be decided during the preparatory period. Please decide by public vote. Decision: The candidates for the Unification Committee will be decided after the standing committees submit a list of names for discussion at the next standing committee meeting on Wednesday. (7) proposing whether to entertain the Beijing press and the Beijing-based reporters of newspapers from Beijing, Shanghai, Hankou, in order to spread publicity and achieve quick results. Please decide by public vote. Decision: First, investigate the Beijing-based reporters of Beijing newspapers, and then choose a date to entertain the reporters. The chairman proposed that the committees submit the proposals to the editing and review department of the museum before the meeting next Wednesday so that they can be included in the agenda.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Random Remarks

Liquidation! Bankruptcy!

— Yafei

The problem is unfolding before us in this way; it seems to be getting more serious! However, those who are intoxicated in the embrace of the metropolis are still enjoying themselves in comfort and pleasure, desperately indulging in the aroma of wine and meat, and anesthetizing themselves. How can they care about these things?

The wave of global economic recession surged for a while. But after the efforts and struggles of the people of various countries, it has finally improved a lot. However, it still tightly shrouds China, even more severely than in the past. Although everyone in China knows that it is subject to external economic aggression and internal war disasters, as well as other heavy oppression. The rural economy is collapsing, and the commercial market is bankrupt. The people are impoverished, and the country is exhausted to the extreme! However, these neighboring powers, eyeing China like tigers, still regard China as a forbidden delicacy; everyone wants to get involved. Recently, the United States is advocating raising the price of silver, intending to dump their surplus products into our country's market. They don't even see that our country's commerce is already struggling with exhausted voices, and the result is still bankruptcy and liquidation!

The banners of year-round big sales and big giveaways are fluttering in front of every store or company, which already symbolizes the general ironclad proof of the decline of our country's market. Although they keep shouting "regardless of cost, unprecedented sacrifice," cheap goods still have to be exchanged for money after all!

At the end of the lunar year, the court authorities received more than 500 business firms that had been applied for sealing by creditors. The court authorities, in consideration of maintaining the appearance of the great Shanghai market, transferred the matter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to find ways to mediate. Unexpectedly, due to the lack of mediation, more than 200 firms have already declared bankruptcy and liquidation on their own. This includes more than 20 silk and satin businesses, more than 10 southern goods businesses, more than 10 money shops, and more than 100 other large and small businesses. And there are still business firms that are about to close but have not yet closed, and those that are about to go bankrupt but have not yet gone bankrupt. I am afraid that in the near future, they will also close their doors one after another!

Looking at the newspapers from various provinces and counties in the interior, the phenomenon of economic recession is no different from that in Shanghai. Taking Huzhou alone, more than 400 business firms have closed down this year due to excessive losses. In Hangzhou, Suzhou, and other places, the number of business firms that have declared liquidation and bankruptcy because they cannot maintain the status quo accounts for two-thirds. A few that are barely struggling temporarily are also in a precarious state. Judging from this situation, according to my observation, by the Dragon Boat Festival of this lunar year, perhaps a large number of business firms will have to prepare to post liquidation notices on their doors.

Our country's intelligent capitalists, seeing the terrifying phenomenon of the commercial future, are all refraining from moving forward, regarding commerce as if it were a dangerous path. Everyone dares not invest in commerce, but instead deposits money in banks or buys securities and public bonds to earn a little interest. Therefore, this makes general merchants feel even more the lack of funds and the inflexibility of financial turnover.

The fact that general stores in Shanghai cannot maintain the status quo is directly due to the oppression of rent, which is indeed a major reason. Therefore, I also advocate that if we want to revive the prosperity of the Shanghai market, we must reduce rent. Reducing rent is a matter of urgent importance at present. Its reasons are most obvious in two aspects: (1) Reducing rent can directly reduce the burden on citizens, and the expenses of stores will also be saved as a result. (2) Indirectly, it can give a blow to capitalists who are engaged in real estate investment, so that they can reduce their delusions of investing in real estate and not cause land prices to rise arbitrarily. Therefore, if we want to save the Shanghai commercial market, the prerequisite is to reduce rent. However, how easy is it to talk about? Those powerful and stubborn industrialists and big landlords are not easy to deal with after all. Moreover, the inside story of the rent reduction movement, it is said, is that the members are also very complicated.

In short, if things continue like this, then I can say that not only is the commercial future of our entire country not optimistic.

An Explanation of Small Families

— Construction

In large cities, the small family is already the organization of the times. But in the interior, it has yet to sprout. Even in the cities, there are still some old-fashioned thinkers who sigh and denounce it, saying that the small family organization is nothing more than a fashionable disease of Westernization, a selfish and self-serving little organization, an act of human degeneration, a base doctrine that deviates from economic principles... From this, we can see that it is still a problem, and that there are people who oppose its establishment.

We believe that an organization, or simply, let's call it a thing, whether it is a good thing or a bad thing; whether it should be opposed or not, we have one condition to determine it, which is to see whether it meets our actual needs. I think this is the best way to evaluate its merits. Here we can examine the essence of the small family. From history, we see the prosperity of tribal times and their decline, which shows that a social organization, or a social system, does not have a perpetual suitability, but will die when it reaches the stage of aging. We can see this in the decline of the Roman Empire; without this explanation, it is difficult to find the reason why such a powerful country would be destroyed. In the family organization, we can also find the same reason. The old large family system, inheriting the remnants of the clan society, flourished. The head of a large family was like a king of a country. He controlled the family's economic power and held the life and death of the entire family. He ruled and controlled everything they did. Under this control, the whole family worked together to produce (the distribution of products was up to the head of the family), and it shone with extraordinary brilliance. But when society develops to a certain stage, the organization changes, and at this time we can see that the brilliance of the large family gradually loses its luster. The position of agriculture has been replaced by industry, the fields are full of machines, and the workers in the fields have become surplus idlers, migrating in groups to industrial areas. Thus, economically, the large family is no longer needed, on the one hand because of the collapse of dispersion, and on the other hand because of the relationship of life. However, it is not the fundamental destruction of the family, but the need for a new organization. Thus, the small family inevitably appears in the development of history.

Because in large families, we know that there are several defects that cannot be concealed: first, there are too few producers and too many non-producers in large families; second, the economic power of large families is in the hands of the head of the family alone, and the family members, even if they devote themselves to production with all their might, cannot secure the comfort of their own and their wives' food and clothing; third, because of economic poverty, the feelings between brothers and sisters-in-law cannot but be opposed; fourth, because marriages are arranged, love cannot be obtained from wives, causing infinite depression in life.

Therefore, we know that this family organization with too many defects cannot continue to exist and must be replaced by small families. The so-called small family is only different from the large family. Its members are only a husband, a wife, and their minor children. Living in modern society, the skills of making a living must be possessed by each individual, because no one has the power to bear the lives of several people, and the organization of the family should be that every family member is responsible for the economy. This is the foundation of the small family. All men and women who want to form a family must have grown up, not only grown up, but also able to maintain their lives independently. Another point is that their union is due to love. From the union of love, we know that first, they can know each other deeply, and they can get deep comfort from each other in life; second, they can endure hardships together and strive for their own happiness. If they say they will both produce, they will both enjoy. There are no idle members who do not produce, and no idle people who do not love each other to divide their interests. When the children grow up, they become the preparatory members of the small family. At this time, in addition to education, they no longer ask for any material rights from their parents' family temple. They cannot but find a job, and after finding a job, they will form a small family.

From this point of view, we know, is this small family a selfish and self-serving little organization, a fashionable disease of Westernization, an act of human degeneration, and a base doctrine that deviates from economic principles? If they are not hot-headed people, they will of course know that this is the error of the opponents. The small family is a system that will inevitably occur in the course of social evolution, and this system is precisely in line with our actual needs, and can stimulate and promote us to step on the road to progress. As for whether this small family organization is in line with modern economic principles, it is even more beyond the comprehension of ordinary people. We know that the consolidation of an organization depends entirely on its economic foundation. It is of course far superior to have each member produce and maintain their lives independently, compared to many members of large families who do not produce and rely on others to live.

A Friend from a Foreign Land

— Wang Ci

The Avenue Joffre at night is like a rainbow, with shops on both sides spewing out light like crazy.

Suddenly, a hand patted my shoulder. When I turned around, I recognized the owner of the hand as Duzjikov—he was a White Russian, my neighbor, selling Evening Posts.

"Where are you going? Mr. Wang."

I smiled at him and shook my head, meaning that I was just wandering around aimlessly!

He looked at me with heavy pupils, a sad smile floating on his lips.

"Duzjikov, didn't you sell newspapers today?"

"Hahahaha," he laughed wildly:

"I have money today! I don't need to sell newspapers today!"

He patted his pocket, where small and large silver coins were fighting.

"Don't you want to add a better piece of clothing, Duzjikov?"

He was stunned, looked at his old aristocratic clothing, and seemed to remember something again, his face darkened; after a while, a bitter smile still floated on the corner of his mouth, and he slowly shook his head:

Page 18

"I don't like to wear that classless clothing!"

I don't know what kind of instigation made him excited, pulled my shoulder, and said earnestly:

"Go! Let's go get drunk!"

The milky white glass door with "BAR" painted on it swallowed us in; the rainbow-like Avenue Joffre left outside the door was stunned.

"Number Three!" Duzjikov and I occupied a glass-topped seat, and casually called out like that.

The white-clothed girl who was called "Number Three" walked over, sat on the remaining stool, and stared at Duzjikov's face! Her face was dim and miserable.

"Oh! Here you are again, Duzjikov, didn't you sell newspapers tonight?" The white-clothed girl had no charm, no coyness, her face was worried:

"Anna, ah! Tonight! Tonight, what I need is not poisonous silver coins, tonight I want to get drunk!"

Anna brought two plates of pork chops and two glasses of scarlet alcohol.

Anna turned her head, her gaze fell on my face, nodded slightly to me, and then asked Duzjikov in fluent English:

"This………………?"

"This is a Chinese man who is in the same situation as us, Mr. Wang; and he is also a writer full of emotions."

Anna nodded to me again and asked me softly in fluent English:

"Where is Mr. Wang's home?"

"No home."

"Where is your lover?"

"No lover."

Duzjikov and I poured the scarlet alcohol into our hearts: one cup, two cups, three cups…

"Anna, dear," Duzjikov raised his very hot face; "Get me another cup!"

Anna was almost crying; she grabbed Duzjikov's arm, her voice trembling:

"My love, stop it! This place is made of money!"

Duzjikov's face became ferocious:

"Anna, Anna, ah! Isn't even alcohol allowed to me in this world?"

Duzjikov shook off Anna's arm, tears welling up in his eyes, and roared.

Anna had no choice but to bring another cup.

"Number Three!" A white man on the left seat shouted like that.

Anna stood up, forced a smile, wanting to go over, but was dragged by Duzjikov, muttering:

"Anna…dear…"

Anna smiled bitterly:

"Duzjikov! This place is made of money!"

Duzjikov watched Anna walk over, watching Anna throw herself into the white man's arms.

He turned his head, and said to me soullessly:

"Do you really have no home?"

"Really."

"Do you really have no lover?"

"Really."

"Ah! Haven't I lost my home; sold the love of my lover?"

To the mouth of the wine glass: "Let's drain this cup!"

Amateur Mailbox

Answers to Several Legal Questions (3)

Mr. Editor:

I have repeatedly read the supplements, and I know that if apprentices have any difficulties, they can ask you, and you will answer them without exception. Therefore, I venture to ask you about my difficult questions, hoping that you will not hesitate to answer them for me.

My uncle passed away in 1923, leaving behind a wife and two daughters. The eldest daughter is now married, and the second daughter is also betrothed to someone else. However, my aunt has always been unrighteous, and two years ago, she had a private affair with another man in Shanghai. Neighbors and relatives all know about it. But because my aunt is unusually fierce, everyone is afraid of her. My father passed away nine years ago, and I am also young, so I have no power to resist. The five acres of ancestral land left behind have all been sold out, and she also wants to sell an ancestral house. I and my relatives did not allow her to sell it, so last year, when the eldest daughter got married, she said as an excuse, "I have no money to buy wine for the wedding, I have no choice but to sell the house." So I spent fifty yuan to pawn it, and wrote a pawn ticket. Now the house ticket is in my aunt's hands. If my aunt uses the house ticket to borrow money in the future, after borrowing, can I refuse to pay it back? Can my aunt's house ticket be invalidated? My aunt is having an affair with another man, what can I do to break away from her, so that she doesn't come to my door? Do I have any rights to the house? Please answer each question in detail. I hope you will reply to me. I respectfully ask for your peace.

Yours sincerely, Dong Yong

Editor's Note:

(1) If there is solid evidence of the field property left by your father, you can order the landlord to return it. As for the pawned house, the owner of the property can still mortgage it for borrowing or sale. The pawnee cannot interfere, but no further pawns may be set.

(2) The nephew has no right to interfere with his aunt's affair.

Husband and Wife (9)

— Yu Mei

The man, smoking a cigarette, glanced at her, then fixed his eyes on the hole of the fire head, watching the black ointment swell up, listening to the sucking sound, and everything around the hole went into the cigarette holder.

Spitting out the last remaining smoke from his mouth, he said,

"It's always hard to say. Last time, I heard Wu Qiantai, the third boss, say a lot to our boss, something about cheap bones hurting the dragon, something about the decline of gold, and also dragged in a lot of imperialism. After all, I don't know what the reason is."

"Is it really the end of the world? It can't be, right."

"It's hard to say, maybe it's this reason. I heard old people say that before the Great Qing Emperor was destroyed, a real person came down to say that the world would be in chaos for thirty years. There are still eight or nine years left. It's really getting harder and harder to live."

"To tell you the truth, when we were girls, the little maids weren't as bad as they are now. Now they all know how to talk about fashion, even fifteen or sixteen-year-old girls are bad, know how to be coquettish. And there are families that rely on this."

"Little girls are bad, but our wallets aren't up to par, so we can only drool."

"You're still so shameless, why don't you look in the mirror to see how old you are."

The two laughed happily for a while, giving each other considerable caresses, the shadows of the two heads merged into one on the top of the tent, and it took a long time to separate. The man's hand was still roaming on the hill, and the woman closed her eyes slightly, letting the man move.

"Third girl, will you still care about me when I have no money in the future?"

"Don't say these tasteless words." She glanced at the man with her eyes rolled back, and her heartbeat quickened.

"I guessed it a long time ago, what you would say in your heart." His hand was still roaming, and his mouth stuck to the woman's cheek.

"What I said in my heart is, 'My third girl only recognizes people, not money. People can buy on credit. Money can't buy everything.'"

The man was happy, and rubbed the woman crazily. The woman sucked on his mouth. Low, soft, tangled, and indistinguishable laughter flickered in the lamplight, swaying the hearts of the two people.

Triumph and passion were boiling in the man's heart, he said, "Third girl, don't worry, no matter how bad I am, I will never forget you. Little darling, put it away a little better, if I have money, would you be willing to leave Xu San and follow me?"

"If you have money, you will forget us. You won't just take the good ones and run away, don't哄me."

"I'm really not 哄ing you. When you go to burn incense on the fifteenth, don't forget to sue for me, and pray to the Bodhisattva to make a fortune."

"Speaking of making a fortune, cough, I had an interesting dream last night! I dreamed that I got a lottery ticket and got a thousand yuan. Strangely, you took away five hundred. Later, the money disappeared again. Dream fortune is lost fortune, is this how the dream is interpreted?"

"Maybe you're going to make a fortune this year. I'm willing to die this life if I meet someone who pays me back."

"You have to die in my arms." The woman looked at him, unable to help laughing in her heart.

"Okay, let's die tonight." The man threw the cigarette stick, indicating that he could remove the smoking set.

Third girl put away everything on the bed. She said that her husband was going home, and asked him to leave. But the man was clever, saying that he had already left her a piece of satin when he was inventorying, which was just right for making a jacket. She said with a smile,

"Looking at your filial piety." Before she finished speaking, she smiled and walked outside the room to latch the door.

Making the bed, she sat down in the corner by the wardrobe. Everything was in infinite silence, only the sound of 　　　　　 in the corner. The man took off his jacket on the table, and had already taken off his shoes and got on the bed. The woman stood up, closed the door, turned down the lamp on the table, put down the curtain, and went into the bed. The sound of lips licking leaked out from the cloth curtain.

[Movie Special

Hollywood's Major Stars' Valuations at the Start of the New Year (3)

— Xi Fu

Now that we've finished talking about the stars at MGM, let's talk about the stars at Paramount. Paramount's most popular star right now is Mae West. Her voluptuous body and seductive movements first revealed her sensuality in "She Done Him Wrong," making people all over the world want to "Go West." Later, she starred in "I'm No Angel," which made people even more crazy. In this regard, in addition to saying that her market value in the securities market has soared to an out-of-control level, many film critics are unable to determine whether this phenomenon is permanent or just a temporary fad, and can only wait for her to release a few more films before seeing.

Bing Crosby was a new development at Paramount in 1933. Her price will definitely rise every time it is auctioned in the securities market. His musical comedy, like "Too Much Harmony," has already established his superior position in the film market. Marlene Dietrich was originally known for her "legs," and later for her "trousers"; although she had so much fresh publicity material, her price has fallen below the baseline in the past year. The biggest reason is that she has made too few films, and her films always feel the same. Someone used to compare her to Garbo, but now they feel that this comparison is too inappropriate. However, she recently starred in a big film called "The Scarlet Empress," and the time for her to restore her original position is probably here.

Another big star whose price has plummeted in 1933 is Maurice Chevalier. This fact is unanimously recognized by filmmakers and film critics. Or he himself also admits this fact, because he has automatically canceled his contract with Paramount and announced that from now on, he must have a script that suits his personality and style before making a new film. Recently, he starred in "Merry Widow" for MGM, which may increase his securities price somewhat.

The rest of Paramount's stars can be briefly mentioned. Sylvia Sidney has almost plummeted. Miriam Hopkins, Richard Arlen, and Fredric March can still maintain their reputation. Carole Lombard and Jack Oakie have made considerable progress. Gary Cooper, Claudette Colbert, and George Raft all saw a significant increase in box office revenue in the past year. The Marx Brothers can still maintain their appeal.

Speaking of the stars of Fox Company, we will first think of Janet Gaynor. She seems to be Hollywood's lucky star forever. Since the success of her "Seventh Heaven," she has steadily been the idol of American movie fans for many years, and until now, her position has not changed at all. Regardless of whether her films are good or bad, many of her worshippers also admit that some of her films are extremely bad, her tens of millions of movie fans will always crowd to buy tickets to see her. So she is still a very reliable collateral in the securities market for movie stars.

Warner Baxter's position is also very stable. His "Paddy the Next Best Thing" and "42nd Street" last year have increased his price in the securities market. Although he is not a heavily promoted actor, his name on the list of actors is the income on the filmmaker's books. (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "The Lost Chord" (兰心，光陆)

— Ling He

Without pretense, this is a sentimental romantic work. It was most prevalent in literature in the eighteenth century, and in film, this trend still remains.

David is a musician who leaves his beloved lover for the sake of art. However, at this time, his lover, Montelin, succumbs to power and marries the Earl. When David returns to the country from the United States five years later, the Earl sees David and Montelin embracing and kissing, and angrily divorces his wife and takes his daughter to Spain. From then on, David went to Spain to duel with the Earl in order to win back the love of his beloved's daughter. The Earl dies, and he is also injured, losing the feeling of playing the piano with his right hand. His daughter, Joan, is taken to the United States, and his lover goes to a monastery to become a nun. Twenty years later, David and Joan meet, and she is already a famous stage actress, and he composes music for her. He and she fall in love from then on. After Joan and David's nephew break off their love due to a misunderstanding, on the eve of the wedding, they learn that Joan is Montelin's daughter, and they try to promote her marriage to his nephew, while he recalls his lover in the dark.

Sentimental romances often make people feel sad and depressed. In this respect, the author of "The Lost Chord" has indeed grasped this atmosphere quite well. Especially when David meets Montelin in the monastery, the mournful piano sound, monotonous in the silent air, can make people weep, everything is in the past, the past is like smoke, David has spent the long years in sad mood. Afterwards, due to the relationship with Montelin's beloved daughter, he once again feels sadness in extreme excitement. In the last mournful sound of the monastery, our protagonist makes people walk out of the theater with a sad and heavy heart.

However, although the director is dealing with a tragedy, the tone of suffering and exile is not as moving as the tone of sadness and depression. I think this is something that should be particularly pointed out. When he writes sad scenes, he often contrasts them with the joy of others. Montelin and David wept, while writing about the Earl and Sharon's flirtation. When Montelin is waiting sadly for David in David's room, he writes about the warm applause and cheers in the theater. David raises a glass to celebrate with Joan, causing Joan's sadness, while writing about the licentious guests singing loudly outdoors, etc. These scenes where human sorrow and joy are originally not connected are even more cruel and terrible in drama.

In addition, we can point out the characteristics of this film from the composition of the picture. Regarding the various scenes in the monastery, in addition to making people feel a sense of holiness and nobility, in the scene of the duel at the Earl's house, the entire composition is due to the stage-like device, which makes people feel nostalgic in this ancient castle.

Of course, this film has its shortcomings. This is not only to say that the scenery of the celebration is too fake, but more importantly, it is too concise. This is not the economy of cutting, but the connection of the picture is too simple and only uses dialogue to explain the plot. This stage play approach is undoubtedly very unsuitable for film. The other things are omitted.

Supplementary Review of "Alice in Wonderland" “Alice in Wonderland” 丨Cathay丨

— Di Ci

Lewis Carroll's famous fairy tale "Alice in Wonderland" has been brought to the screen. It was shown at Cathay during the Chinese New Year. Although it didn't cause a sensation like "Don Quixote," it still attracted a lot of attention.

I don't deny that children, like adults, need spiritual nourishment; nor do I deny that there are many fantasies in children's minds; at the same time, they often personify certain things. However, in any case, I always feel that in the name of children's literature, it is wrong to give children all kinds of empty stories without principle, and not to give them correct guidance based on their fantasies. China has never paid attention to children's literature. Many people are currently working hard to create children's literature, but what we see is more poison than tonic. This is the first impression I had when watching "Alice in Wonderland."

Carroll was a famous mathematician. He used his qualifications as a mathematician to write children's stories, so what "Alice in Wonderland" first gives children is logic and rich knowledge. This is why "Alice in Wonderland" has become a favorite of modern people, and it is not accidental. But "Alice in Wonderland" is, after all, an old fairy tale, and Carroll is sometimes confused by his own fantasies and prejudices. Therefore, in "Alice in Wonderland," we can only slightly see his dissatisfaction with reality, and there is not much reform significance here. Of course, people will defend him by saying that fairy tales are originally meant to organize children's emotions secretly, but what we need to pay attention to is what is used to organize them? And what kind of things are they organized into? Therefore, there is no question that "Alice in Wonderland" is not the novel and film that is currently needed.

The "Alice" on the screen is not much different from the "Alice" in the book, and the performance of many characters also follows the illustrations in the book. So, if we watch this film, even if we haven't read "Alice," it doesn't matter, because it uses extremely appropriate because it is a fairy tale, the director focuses on "fun." The "fun" here is not the kind of nonsense found in slapstick comedies. From the costumes to the movements, it already gives us fun, especially the elegant and light movements of several animals. Many of the heads have masks, so facial expressions are very lacking. The others are quite remarkable. At least in scenes such as going to heaven and earth, the movie expresses its unique function even more. The special use of time and space can only be done by movies.

"It is difficult to draw dogs and horses" because everyone has seen dogs and horses. "It is easy to draw gods and monsters" because no one has seen gods and monsters. Where should we start to criticize everything in "Alice in Wonderland" technically? We can only make general comments.

(Editor's note: This article was delayed until today due to the backlog of manuscripts after the Spring Festival holiday.)

### An Accidental Anti-Hitler Film

— Fu Xi

Since the leader of the National Socialist Party in Germany, Hitler, became Chancellor, he has greatly suppressed the Jews in the country, causing them to lose their jobs and property, and become homeless. Perhaps only the Jews who have suffered the misfortune know the tragic situation. Originally, since the rise of National Socialism in Germany, foreign films have suffered a major blow because they were difficult to import. Unexpectedly, Hollywood has recently produced a film full of anti-National Socialism, and it is feared that American films will be even more envied by the German government authorities. The film stars the big star George Arliss and is called "The House of Rothschild." Rothschild is the largest Jewish financial group in Europe, and its family's banks are spread all over Europe. George Arliss's film depicts the history between that great financial group and various governments. One section describes how, in the most prosperous era, the family "ordered" the Prussian government to restore German citizenship to Jews. Because the Prussian government wanted a large loan, it had no choice but to obey the financial group's instructions and order the restoration of German citizenship to all Jews. Although this story is a historical fact, it coincides with current events, as if satirizing the current German government, which will have to yield to Jewish financial groups due to poverty. Of course, the producers in the United States are doing their best to argue that the film has no malicious propaganda, but how can they get the understanding of the German authorities?

"Raging Tide of the China Sea" Passes Censorship and Will Be Released

Since the opening of Yi Hua Film Company, it has caused a lot of speculation from the outside world because it has not yet released any works. However, I dare say that this is a good phenomenon for Yi Hua. You must understand that other people's speculation is attention to oneself, then under the attention of others, you will naturally work harder to engage in work.

Finally, Yue Feng's "Raging Tide of the China Sea" was produced under such circumstances.

"Raging Tide of the China Sea" has been passed by the Nanjing Film Censorship Board and can be released in Shanghai recently. The film has profound performances, flexible shots, and interesting small movements. The strongman Cha Rui Long changed his style and performed calmly, which is indeed extraordinary. Yuan Meiyun's liveliness and Wang Yin's excitement can even more stimulate people's hearts. Indeed, everything in "Raging Tide of the China Sea" is extraordinary.

Of course, Yi Hua Film Company is showing the facts to people.

Film Novel

Film Novel Iron-Blooded Rouge (1)

— Long Geng

Starring Wang Yuanlong, Fan Xuepeng, and Tang Jie Produced by Tianyi

The tiger in the zoo was exerting its strength to chew on the large piece of beef, a gift from Brigade Commander Gao Yan.

Gao Yan had an insidious face, with a monocle covering his left eye. The powerful gaze shot out from behind the lens, making him seem strange and frightening. The mustache on his lips was twisted powerfully. His teeth, like the tiger in the cage, protruded from his lips, as if he wanted to eat people.

Li Xuejuan, the wife of Battalion Commander Lin Zhenxiao, was strolling in the zoo with Shen, the wife of Zhenxiao's friend Lu Yuanfu. Unfortunately, Li Xuejuan's beautiful and lovely expression was seen by the lecherous Gao Yan, and a kind of ambition to "possess her" filled his chest at the same time. Therefore, he basely approached her.

Adjutant Ma Yunbiao was a friend of Lu Yuanfu and also knew that Li Xuejuan was Lin Zhenxiao's wife. Therefore, Gao Yan, who was full of thoughts of possessing Li Xuejuan, delegated the responsibility of "matching them up" to Ma Yunbiao.

Ma Yunbiao went to Lu Yuanfu's house, preparing to unload the responsibility of "matching them up" to Lu Yuanfu. Lu Yuanfu was an honest man, and he understood that Zhenxiao was his friend. In the friendship between friends, he should not erase his conscience to do this base and immoral deed. Therefore, he always could not allow it, no matter what "official" was used to seduce him. However, the fire of vanity burned Shen's heart. "Official," what a noble and glorious term. What does a friend count for! Finally, desire won, and she snatched the responsibility to bear.

Of course, Li Xuejuan did not understand that someone was hunting her body for fame and fortune. She only understood to serve her husband loyally. Originally, their couple was full of sweet and joyful vitality. They only felt that he was the one who could grow old with her forever. Of course, she was him in his eyes, but who would have thought? Misfortune was beginning right before their eyes.

Shen knocked on the door and came in, inviting Xuejuan to eat at her house, saying that many relatives were waiting. Although Xuejuan wanted to cook for her beloved husband, her husband Zhenxiao, for the sake of his friendship with his friend, agreed with Shen's words and went to her house. So, Xuejuan went. (To be continued)
